// âš  LÆ¯U Ã QUAN TRá»ŒNG:
//   "global using Alias = Type" KHÃ”NG há»— trá»£ type-arguments (e.g. Alias<T>)
//   â†’ KHÃ”NG dÃ¹ng kiá»ƒu Ä‘Ã³. Chá»‰ import namespace bÃ¬nh thÆ°á»ng nhÆ° bÃªn dÆ°á»›i.

// Nhá» dÃ²ng nÃ y, má»i file trong project Ä‘á»u dÃ¹ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c Task<T>

global using System.Threading.Tasks;
namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs
{
    // =====================================================
    // DTO (Data Transfer Object) â€“ Ä‘á»‘i tÆ°á»£ng truyá»n dá»¯ liá»‡u giá»¯a cÃ¡c táº§ng
    //
    // Táº¡i sao cáº§n DTO thay vÃ¬ truyá»n Entity tháº³ng?
    //   Entity chá»©a táº¥t cáº£ cá»™t DB (ká»ƒ cáº£ PasswordHash, CreatedAt...)
    //   DTO chá»‰ chá»©a Ä‘Ãºng dá»¯ liá»‡u táº§ng trÃªn cáº§n biáº¿t
    //   â†’ an toÃ n hÆ¡n, giáº£m coupling giá»¯a táº§ng
    // =====================================================

    /// <summary>
    /// Káº¿t quáº£ tráº£ vá» sau khi gá»i IAuthService.LoginAsync().
    ///
    /// DÃ¹ng Result Pattern thay vÃ¬ throw Exception cho lá»—i nghiá»‡p vá»¥:
    ///   - Form dá»… kiá»ƒm tra: if (!result.Success) { lblError.Text = result.ErrorMessage; }
    ///   - KhÃ´ng cáº§n try-catch cho lá»—i "sai máº­t kháº©u" (Ä‘Ã¢y khÃ´ng pháº£i exception)
    ///   - Exception chá»‰ dÃ nh cho lá»—i háº¡ táº§ng (DB máº¥t káº¿t ná»‘i, ...)
    /// </summary>
    public class LoginResult
    {
        public bool   Success      { get; init; }
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; init; } // null khi thÃ nh cÃ´ng
        public UserSessionDto? User { get; init; } // null khi tháº¥t báº¡i

        // Factory methods â€“ táº¡o káº¿t quáº£ rÃµ nghÄ©a, khÃ´ng new trá»±c tiáº¿p
        public static LoginResult Ok(UserSessionDto user)
            => new() { Success = true, User = user };

        public static LoginResult Fail(string message)
            => new() { Success = false, ErrorMessage = message };
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// ThÃ´ng tin user cáº§n thiáº¿t sau khi Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p â€“ lÆ°u vÃ o AppSession.
    ///
    /// Chá»§ Ä‘á»™ng KHÃ”NG cÃ³ PasswordHash Ä‘á»ƒ:
    ///   - KhÃ´ng vÃ´ tÃ¬nh lá»™ hash ra Form/UI
    ///   - Giáº£m dá»¯ liá»‡u khÃ´ng cáº§n thiáº¿t trong bá»™ nhá»›
    /// </summary>
    public class UserSessionDto
    {
        public int    Id         { get; init; }
        public string Username   { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string FullName   { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string Email      { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string? AvatarPath { get; init; }

        // Danh sÃ¡ch tÃªn role: ["Admin"], ["Manager"], ["Developer"]
        // DÃ¹ng Ä‘á»ƒ kiá»ƒm tra quyá»n trong AppSession (IsAdmin, IsManager...)
        public List<string> Roles { get; init; } = new();
    }
}

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    public class Project
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        [Required, MaxLength(200)]
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [MaxLength(2000)]
        public string? Description { get; set; }

        // ---- KhÃ¡ch hÃ ng ----
        public int? CustomerId { get; set; }
        public Customer? Customer { get; set; }

        // ---- NgÆ°á»i sá»Ÿ há»¯u / PM ----
        public int OwnerId { get; set; }
        public User Owner { get; set; } = null!;

        // ---- Timeline ----
        public DateOnly StartDate { get; set; }
        public DateOnly? PlannedEndDate { get; set; }
        public DateOnly? ActualEndDate { get; set; }

        // ---- NgÃ¢n sÃ¡ch ----
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(18,2)")]
        public decimal Budget { get; set; } = 0;

        // ---- Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i & Æ¯u tiÃªn ----
        /// <summary>NotStarted | InProgress | OnHold | Completed | Cancelled</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(30)]
        public string Status { get; set; } = "NotStarted";

        /// <summary>1=Low | 2=Medium | 3=High | 4=Critical</summary>
        public byte Priority { get; set; } = 2;

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        public DateTime UpdatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        /* ================= RELATIONSHIPS ================= */
        public ICollection<TaskItem> Tasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();
        public ICollection<ProjectMember> Members { get; set; } = new List<ProjectMember>();
        public ICollection<Expense> Expenses { get; set; } = new List<Expense>();

        /* ================= COMPUTED (khÃ´ng map DB) ================= */
        [NotMapped]
        public decimal TotalExpense => Expenses?.Sum(e => e.Amount) ?? 0;

        [NotMapped]
        public int ProgressPercent
        {
            get
            {
                var rootTasks = Tasks?.Where(t => t.ParentTaskId == null).ToList();
                if (rootTasks == null || rootTasks.Count == 0) return 0;
                return (int)rootTasks.Average(t => t.ProgressPercent);
            }
        }
    }
}

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// CÃ´ng viá»‡c (Task) trong dá»± Ã¡n.
    /// 
    /// Workflow 10 tráº¡ng thÃ¡i:
    ///   CREATED â†’ ASSIGNED â†’ IN-PROGRESS â†’ REVIEW-1 â†’ REVIEW-2 â†’ APPROVED â†’ IN-TEST â†’ RESOLVED â†’ CLOSED
    ///                             â†‘             â†“          â†“                     â†“
    ///                             â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ FAILED â†â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜â†â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
    /// 
    /// Má»—i giai Ä‘oáº¡n cÃ³ ngÆ°á»i phá»¥ trÃ¡ch riÃªng:
    ///   - AssignedTo: ngÆ°á»i lÃ m task (Developer)
    ///   - Reviewer1: ngÆ°á»i review láº§n 1 (peer/team lead)
    ///   - Reviewer2: ngÆ°á»i review láº§n 2 (senior/architect)
    ///   - Tester: ngÆ°á»i kiá»ƒm thá»­ (QA)
    /// 
    /// Luá»“ng gÃ¡n ngÆ°á»i:
    ///   Táº¡o task â†’ gÃ¡n Assignee
    ///   Assignee xong â†’ chuyá»ƒn REVIEW-1 + gÃ¡n Reviewer1
    ///   Reviewer1 pass â†’ chuyá»ƒn REVIEW-2 + gÃ¡n Reviewer2
    ///   Reviewer2 pass â†’ APPROVED â†’ IN-TEST + gÃ¡n Tester
    ///   Báº¥t ká»³ ai (Reviewer1/2, Tester) reject â†’ FAILED â†’ Assignee sá»­a láº¡i
    /// </summary>
    public class TaskItem
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TiÃªu Ä‘á» cÃ´ng viá»‡c (báº¯t buá»™c, tá»‘i Ä‘a 200 kÃ½ tá»±).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(200)]
        public string Title { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>MÃ´ táº£ chi tiáº¿t cÃ´ng viá»‡c (tÃ¹y chá»n, tá»‘i Ä‘a 2000 kÃ½ tá»±).</summary>
        [MaxLength(2000)]
        public string? Description { get; set; }

        /// <summary>ÄÃ¡nh dáº¥u task Ä‘Ã£ hoÃ n thÃ nh (tá»± Ä‘á»™ng set khi ProgressPercent = 100).</summary>
        public bool IsCompleted { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Pháº§n trÄƒm hoÃ n thÃ nh: 0â€“100. Khi = 100 â†’ IsCompleted = true.</summary>
        [Range(0, 100)]
        public byte ProgressPercent { get; set; } = 0;

        /// <summary>Sá»‘ giá» Æ°á»›c tÃ­nh Ä‘á»ƒ hoÃ n thÃ nh task.</summary>
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(6,1)")]
        public decimal? EstimatedHours { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Sá»‘ giá» thá»±c táº¿ Ä‘Ã£ lÃ m.</summary>
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(6,1)")]
        public decimal? ActualHours { get; set; }

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
        public DateTime UpdatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        /// <summary>Háº¡n chÃ³t hoÃ n thÃ nh task.</summary>
        public DateTime? DueDate { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Thá»i Ä‘iá»ƒm task Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘Ã¡nh dáº¥u hoÃ n thÃ nh (status = RESOLVED/CLOSED).</summary>
        public DateTime? CompletedAt { get; set; }

        /* ================= RELATIONSHIPS ================= */

        /// <summary>Dá»± Ã¡n chá»©a task nÃ y.</summary>
        public int ProjectId { get; set; }
        public Project Project { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>Task cha (há»— trá»£ sub-task lá»“ng nhau, null = task gá»‘c).</summary>
        public int? ParentTaskId { get; set; }
        public TaskItem? ParentTask { get; set; }
        public ICollection<TaskItem> SubTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>NgÆ°á»i táº¡o task.</summary>
        public int CreatedById { get; set; }
        public User CreatedBy { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>NgÆ°á»i Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao thá»±c hiá»‡n task (Developer chÃ­nh).</summary>
        public int? AssignedToId { get; set; }
        public User? AssignedTo { get; set; }

        // â”€â”€ GD3: Workflow Review & Test â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// NgÆ°á»i review láº§n 1 (peer review / team lead).
        /// ÄÆ°á»£c gÃ¡n khi Assignee chuyá»ƒn task sang REVIEW-1.
        /// </summary>
        public int? Reviewer1Id { get; set; }
        public User? Reviewer1 { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// NgÆ°á»i review láº§n 2 (senior developer / architect).
        /// ÄÆ°á»£c gÃ¡n khi Reviewer1 approve vÃ  chuyá»ƒn sang REVIEW-2.
        /// </summary>
        public int? Reviewer2Id { get; set; }
        public User? Reviewer2 { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// NgÆ°á»i kiá»ƒm thá»­ (QA / Tester).
        /// ÄÆ°á»£c gÃ¡n khi Reviewer2 approve vÃ  chuyá»ƒn sang IN-TEST.
        /// </summary>
        public int? TesterId { get; set; }
        public User? Tester { get; set; }

        // â”€â”€ Lookup tables â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>Má»©c Ä‘á»™ Æ°u tiÃªn (Low / Medium / High / Critical).</summary>
        public int PriorityId { get; set; }
        public Priority Priority { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i hiá»‡n táº¡i trong workflow 10 bÆ°á»›c.</summary>
        public int StatusId { get; set; }
        public Status Status { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>PhÃ¢n loáº¡i task (Bug / Feature / Improvement / Research / Testing).</summary>
        public int CategoryId { get; set; }
        public Category Category { get; set; } = null!;

        // â”€â”€ Collections â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>Danh sÃ¡ch bÃ¬nh luáº­n trÃªn task.</summary>
        public ICollection<Comment> Comments { get; set; } = new List<Comment>();

        /// <summary>Danh sÃ¡ch file Ä‘Ã­nh kÃ¨m.</summary>
        public ICollection<Attachment> Attachments { get; set; } = new List<Attachment>();

        /// <summary>Danh sÃ¡ch tag gáº¯n trÃªn task.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskTag> TaskTags { get; set; } = new List<TaskTag>();
    }

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// TÃ i khoáº£n ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng trong há»‡ thá»‘ng.
    /// Má»™t user cÃ³ thá»ƒ Ä‘Ã³ng nhiá»u vai trÃ² trÃªn task: Assignee, Reviewer, Tester.
    /// </summary>
    public class User
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TÃªn Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p (unique, dÃ¹ng lÃ m khÃ³a nghiá»‡p vá»¥).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(50)]
        public string Username { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Há» vÃ  tÃªn Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§.</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(100)]
        public string FullName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Email (unique).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(100)]
        public string Email { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Máº­t kháº©u Ä‘Ã£ hash báº±ng BCrypt (WorkFactor 12).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(256)]
        public string PasswordHash { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [MaxLength(20)]
        public string? Phone { get; set; }

        [MaxLength(255)]
        public string? AvatarPath { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TÃ i khoáº£n active hay bá»‹ vÃ´ hiá»‡u hÃ³a (soft delete).</summary>
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
        public DateTime? LastLogin { get; set; }

        /* ================= RELATIONSHIPS ================= */

        /// <summary>Danh sÃ¡ch role cá»§a user (Admin / Manager / Developer).</summary>
        public ICollection<UserRole> UserRoles { get; set; } = new List<UserRole>();

        /// <summary>Dá»± Ã¡n user lÃ m Owner/PM.</summary>
        public ICollection<Project> OwnedProjects { get; set; } = new List<Project>();

        /// <summary>Dá»± Ã¡n user tham gia (qua báº£ng ProjectMembers).</summary>
        public ICollection<ProjectMember> ProjectMemberships { get; set; } = new List<ProjectMember>();

        /// <summary>Task do user táº¡o.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> CreatedTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>Task Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao cho user thá»±c hiá»‡n.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> AssignedTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        // â”€â”€ GD3: Workflow Review & Test â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>Task user lÃ m Reviewer láº§n 1.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> Review1Tasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>Task user lÃ m Reviewer láº§n 2.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> Review2Tasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>Task user lÃ m Tester.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> TesterTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>BÃ¬nh luáº­n cá»§a user.</summary>
        public ICollection<Comment> Comments { get; set; } = new List<Comment>();

        /// <summary>Chi phÃ­ do user táº¡o.</summary>
        public ICollection<Expense> CreatedExpenses { get; set; } = new List<Expense>();
    }

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Táº­p trung logic hash/verify máº­t kháº©u báº±ng BCrypt.
    ///
    /// Táº¡i sao BCrypt thay vÃ¬ SHA-256?
    ///   SHA-256: thuáº­t toÃ¡n hash nhanh, GPU cÃ³ thá»ƒ thá»­ 10 tá»· hash/giÃ¢y â†’ dá»… brute-force
    ///   BCrypt:  cá»‘ tÃ¬nh cháº­m (~300ms/hash), cÃ³ cost factor Ä‘iá»u chá»‰nh Ä‘Æ°á»£c
    ///            tá»± sinh salt ngáº«u nhiÃªn cho má»—i password â†’ chá»‘ng rainbow table
    ///
    /// Táº¡i sao tÃ¡ch ra Helper riÃªng?
    ///   AuthService vÃ  UserService Ä‘á»u cáº§n hash/verify
    ///   â†’ Ä‘áº·t 1 chá»— trÃ¡nh duplicate code, dá»… Ä‘á»•i thuáº­t toÃ¡n sau nÃ y
    /// </summary>
    public static class PasswordHelper
    {
        // WorkFactor 12 = 2^12 = 4096 vÃ²ng láº·p ná»™i bá»™ â†’ ~300ms trÃªn CPU thÃ´ng thÆ°á»ng
        // TÄƒng lÃªn 13-14 náº¿u server máº¡nh hÆ¡n (má»—i +1 tÄƒng gáº¥p Ä‘Ã´i thá»i gian hash)
        private const int WorkFactor = 12;

        /// <summary>
        /// Hash máº­t kháº©u báº±ng BCrypt. Salt ngáº«u nhiÃªn Ä‘Æ°á»£c táº¡o tá»± Ä‘á»™ng,
        /// nhÃºng vÃ o trong chuá»—i hash â†’ khÃ´ng cáº§n lÆ°u salt riÃªng.
        /// </summary>
        public static string Hash(string plainPassword)
            => BCrypt.Net.BCrypt.HashPassword(plainPassword, WorkFactor);

        /// <summary>
        /// XÃ¡c minh máº­t kháº©u nháº­p vÃ o vá»›i hash Ä‘Ã£ lÆ°u trong DB.
        /// BCrypt tá»± extract salt tá»« hash â†’ truyá»n vÃ o Ä‘Ãºng 2 tham sá»‘ lÃ  Ä‘á»§.
        /// </summary>
        public static bool Verify(string plainPassword, string hashedPassword)
        {
            try
            {
                return BCrypt.Net.BCrypt.Verify(plainPassword, hashedPassword);
            }
            catch
            {
                // Báº¯t trÆ°á»ng há»£p hash format cÅ© (SHA-256) váº«n cÃ²n trong DB
                // â†’ tráº£ false thay vÃ¬ crash app
                return false;
            }
        }
    }
}
using System.Net.Mail;
using System.Text.RegularExpressions;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Táº­p trung toÃ n bá»™ quy táº¯c validate dÃ¹ng chung cho cÃ¡c Service.
    /// Äáº·t 1 chá»— Ä‘á»ƒ khi thay Ä‘á»•i quy táº¯c chá»‰ sá»­a á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y, Ã¡p dá»¥ng toÃ n app.
    /// </summary>
    public static class ValidationHelper
    {
        /// <summary>Máº­t kháº©u há»£p lá»‡: tá»‘i thiá»ƒu 6 kÃ½ tá»±, khÃ´ng chá»‰ khoáº£ng tráº¯ng.</summary>
        public static bool IsPasswordStrong(string password)
            => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(password) && password.Length >= 6;

        /// <summary>Email há»£p lá»‡ theo chuáº©n RFC (dÃ¹ng MailAddress Ä‘á»ƒ parse).</summary>
        public static bool IsValidEmail(string email)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(email)) return false;
            try
            {
                var addr = new MailAddress(email);
                return addr.Address == email.Trim();
            }
            catch { return false; }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Username há»£p lá»‡: 3-50 kÃ½ tá»±, chá»‰ chá»¯ cÃ¡i, sá»‘ vÃ  dáº¥u gáº¡ch dÆ°á»›i.
        /// Regex: ^[a-zA-Z0-9_]{3,50}$
        /// </summary>
        public static bool IsValidUsername(string username)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(username)) return false;
            return Regex.IsMatch(username, @"^[a-zA-Z0-9_]{3,50}$");
        }
    }
}

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Generic repository interface â€“ táº¥t cáº£ repository Ä‘á»u káº¿ thá»«a interface nÃ y.
    /// Ãp dá»¥ng Repository Pattern: tÃ¡ch biá»‡t logic truy cáº­p dá»¯ liá»‡u khá»i business logic.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">Kiá»ƒu entity (User, Project, TaskItem, ...)</typeparam>
    public interface IRepository<T> where T : class
    {
        /// <summary>Láº¥y 1 báº£n ghi theo khÃ³a chÃ­nh. Tráº£ vá» null náº¿u khÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y.</summary>
        Task<T?> GetByIdAsync(int id);

        /// <summary>Láº¥y toÃ n bá»™ danh sÃ¡ch. DÃ¹ng GetPagedAsync náº¿u dá»¯ liá»‡u lá»›n.</summary>
        Task<List<T>> GetAllAsync();

        /// <summary>ThÃªm má»›i 1 báº£n ghi vÃ o database.</summary>
        Task AddAsync(T entity);

        /// <summary>Cáº­p nháº­t 1 báº£n ghi Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i.</summary>
        Task UpdateAsync(T entity);

        /// <summary>XÃ³a báº£n ghi theo ID (hard delete hoáº·c soft delete tÃ¹y repository).</summary>
        Task DeleteAsync(int id);
    }
}

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Interface cho Task Repository â€“ trung tÃ¢m cá»§a há»‡ thá»‘ng GD4.
    ///
    /// GD4 bá»• sung so vá»›i GD1/GD3:
    ///   - GetByIdWithDetailsAsync: eager load Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§ cho frmTaskEdit
    ///   - GetByReviewerAsync / GetByTesterAsync: cho mÃ n hÃ¬nh Review/Test
    ///   - UpdateStatusAsync: chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i workflow 10 bÆ°á»›c
    ///   - GetLookupDataAsync: láº¥y Priority, Status, Category 1 láº§n cho dropdown
    /// </summary>
    public interface ITaskRepository : IRepository<TaskItem>
    {
        // â”€â”€ Truy váº¥n Ä‘Æ¡n â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// Láº¥y task kÃ¨m toÃ n bá»™ navigation properties.
        /// DÃ¹ng cho frmTaskEdit (cáº§n hiá»ƒn thá»‹ Priority, Status, Category, User, SubTasks).
        /// </summary>
        Task<TaskItem?> GetByIdWithDetailsAsync(int taskId);

        // â”€â”€ PhÃ¢n trang + lá»c Ä‘a tiÃªu chÃ­ â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// PhÃ¢n trang + lá»c káº¿t há»£p nhiá»u tiÃªu chÃ­ (IQueryable filter chain).
        /// Táº¥t cáº£ tham sá»‘ nullable = tÃ¹y chá»n, chá»‰ WHERE khi cÃ³ giÃ¡ trá»‹.
        /// Tráº£ vá» (Items, TotalCount) Ä‘á»ƒ tÃ­nh sá»‘ trang á»Ÿ UI.
        /// </summary>
        Task<(List<TaskItem> Items, int TotalCount)> GetPagedAsync(
            int page,
            int pageSize,
            int?    projectId       = null,
            int?    assignedToId    = null,
            int?    statusId        = null,
            int?    priorityId      = null,
            int?    categoryId      = null,
            string? searchKeyword   = null);

        // â”€â”€ Truy váº¥n theo ngÆ°á»i phá»¥ trÃ¡ch â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// Task chÆ°a hoÃ n thÃ nh Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao cho developer (mÃ n hÃ¬nh "CÃ´ng viá»‡c cá»§a tÃ´i").
        /// Sáº¯p xáº¿p: DueDate tÄƒng dáº§n (gáº§n deadline lÃªn Ä‘áº§u).
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetAssignedToUserAsync(int userId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Ä‘ang chá» review láº§n 1 bá»Ÿi reviewer chá»‰ Ä‘á»‹nh.
        /// Status pháº£i lÃ  REVIEW-1.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetByReviewer1Async(int reviewer1Id);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Ä‘ang chá» review láº§n 2 bá»Ÿi reviewer chá»‰ Ä‘á»‹nh.
        /// Status pháº£i lÃ  REVIEW-2.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetByReviewer2Async(int reviewer2Id);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Ä‘ang chá» test bá»Ÿi tester chá»‰ Ä‘á»‹nh.
        /// Status pháº£i lÃ  IN-TEST.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetByTesterAsync(int testerId);

        // â”€â”€ Truy váº¥n theo dá»± Ã¡n â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// Táº¥t cáº£ task cá»§a 1 dá»± Ã¡n.
        /// includeSubTasks = false â†’ chá»‰ láº¥y task gá»‘c (ParentTaskId == null).
        /// Sáº¯p xáº¿p: Priority DESC â†’ DueDate ASC.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetByProjectAsync(int projectId, bool includeSubTasks = false);

        // â”€â”€ Cáº£nh bÃ¡o / Dashboard â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>Task Ä‘Ã£ quÃ¡ háº¡n (DueDate &lt; Now vÃ  chÆ°a hoÃ n thÃ nh).</summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetOverdueAsync();

        /// <summary>Task sáº¯p Ä‘áº¿n háº¡n trong N ngÃ y tá»›i (máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh 7 ngÃ y).</summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetDueSoonAsync(int days = 7);

        // â”€â”€ Cáº­p nháº­t tá»‘i Æ°u (khÃ´ng cáº§n load entity) â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// Cáº­p nháº­t tiáº¿n Ä‘á»™ % â€” tá»± Ä‘á»™ng set IsCompleted, CompletedAt, vÃ  StatusId.
        ///   progress = 100  â†’ IsCompleted = true,  CompletedAt = Now, StatusId = RESOLVED
        ///   progress &lt; 100  â†’ IsCompleted = false, CompletedAt = null  (má»Ÿ láº¡i náº¿u nháº§m)
        /// DÃ¹ng ExecuteUpdateAsync â€” khÃ´ng cáº§n SELECT entity trÆ°á»›c.
        /// </summary>
        Task UpdateProgressAsync(int taskId, byte progressPercent, int resolvedStatusId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i workflow â€” chá»‰ update StatusId + UpdatedAt.
        /// DÃ¹ng ExecuteUpdateAsync â€” khÃ´ng load entity.
        /// </summary>
        Task UpdateStatusAsync(int taskId, int newStatusId);

        /// <summary>
        /// GÃ¡n ngÆ°á»i review / tester vÃ o task Ä‘á»“ng thá»i chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i.
        /// DÃ¹ng ExecuteUpdateAsync â€” 1 round-trip duy nháº¥t.
        /// </summary>
        Task AssignReviewerAsync(int taskId, int? reviewer1Id, int? reviewer2Id, int? testerId, int newStatusId);

        // â”€â”€ Thá»‘ng kÃª cho Dashboard â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// Äáº¿m task theo Status trong 1 dá»± Ã¡n.
        /// GroupBy trá»±c tiáº¿p trÃªn DB â†’ tráº£ vá» Dictionary (Status.Name â†’ Count).
        /// </summary>
        Task<Dictionary<string, int>> GetStatusSummaryByProjectAsync(int projectId);

        // â”€â”€ Lookup data cho dropdown â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>Láº¥y táº¥t cáº£ Status (10 bÆ°á»›c), sáº¯p theo DisplayOrder.</summary>
        Task<List<Status>> GetAllStatusesAsync();

        /// <summary>Láº¥y táº¥t cáº£ Priority (4 má»©c), sáº¯p theo Level.</summary>
        Task<List<Priority>> GetAllPrioritiesAsync();

        /// <summary>Láº¥y táº¥t cáº£ Category (Bug/Feature/...).</summary>
        Task<List<Category>> GetAllCategoriesAsync();

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Interface cho Task Service â€“ nghiá»‡p vá»¥ quáº£n lÃ½ cÃ´ng viá»‡c GD4.
    ///
    /// GD4 bá»• sung so vá»›i GD1/GD3:
    ///   - CreateTaskAsync / UpdateTaskAsync: validate Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§
    ///   - UpdateProgressAsync: tá»± chuyá»ƒn Status â†’ RESOLVED khi progress = 100
    ///   - UpdateStatusAsync: chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i workflow 10 bÆ°á»›c vá»›i validate
    ///   - GetLookupDataAsync: láº¥y Priority, Status, Category cho dropdown frmTaskEdit
    ///   - GetTasksForReviewerAsync / GetTasksForTesterAsync: cho mÃ n hÃ¬nh Review/Test
    /// </summary>

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Auth
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Triá»ƒn khai IAuthService â€“ xÃ¡c thá»±c ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng (Login).
    ///
    /// Luá»“ng Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p:
    ///   1. Validate username/password khÃ´ng rá»—ng
    ///   2. TÃ¬m user trong DB (chá»‰ user active)
    ///   3. Verify BCrypt password qua PasswordHelper
    ///   4. Load danh sÃ¡ch Roles Ä‘á»ƒ phÃ¢n quyá»n
    ///   5. Map User â†’ UserSessionDto (khÃ´ng expose PasswordHash)
    ///   6. UpdateLastLogin fire-and-forget (khÃ´ng block UI)
    ///   7. Tráº£ LoginResult.Ok hoáº·c LoginResult.Fail
    ///
    /// DÃ¹ng Result Pattern (LoginResult) thay vÃ¬ throw Exception
    /// cho lá»—i nghiá»‡p vá»¥ â†’ Form xá»­ lÃ½ gá»n hÆ¡n, khÃ´ng cáº§n try-catch.
    /// </summary>
    public class AuthService : IAuthService
    {
        private readonly IUserRepository _userRepo;

        // Inject IUserRepository qua constructor (DI Container cung cáº¥p)
        public AuthService(IUserRepository userRepo) => _userRepo = userRepo;

        public async Task<LoginResult> LoginAsync(string username, string password)
        {
            // --- BÆ°á»›c 1: Validate Ä‘áº§u vÃ o (guard clauses) ---
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(username))
                return LoginResult.Fail("âš  Vui lÃ²ng nháº­p tÃªn Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p.");

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(password))
                return LoginResult.Fail("âš  Vui lÃ²ng nháº­p máº­t kháº©u.");

            // --- BÆ°á»›c 2: TÃ¬m user trong DB ---
            // GetByUsernameAsync chá»‰ tráº£ user cÃ³ IsActive = true
            var user = await _userRepo.GetByUsernameAsync(username.Trim());

            // --- BÆ°á»›c 3: Verify BCrypt password ---
            // DÃ¹ng thÃ´ng bÃ¡o chung cho cáº£ 2 trÆ°á»ng há»£p sai username / sai password
            // â†’ trÃ¡nh tiáº¿t lá»™ username cÃ³ tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng khÃ´ng (security)
            if (user == null || !PasswordHelper.Verify(password, user.PasswordHash))
                return LoginResult.Fail("âš  TÃªn Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p hoáº·c máº­t kháº©u khÃ´ng Ä‘Ãºng.");

            // --- BÆ°á»›c 4: Load Roles Ä‘á»ƒ phÃ¢n quyá»n (eager load) ---
            var userWithRoles = await _userRepo.GetWithRolesAsync(user.Id);
            if (userWithRoles == null)
                return LoginResult.Fail("âš  KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº£i thÃ´ng tin quyá»n. Vui lÃ²ng thá»­ láº¡i.");

            // --- BÆ°á»›c 5: Map â†’ DTO (khÃ´ng tráº£ User entity thÃ´ ra ngoÃ i Service) ---
            var dto = UserSessionMapper.ToDto(userWithRoles);

            // --- BÆ°á»›c 6: Cáº­p nháº­t LastLogin (fire-and-forget, khÃ´ng await) ---
            // _ = bá» qua Task tráº£ vá», khÃ´ng block thread UI
            _ = _userRepo.UpdateLastLoginAsync(user.Id);

            return LoginResult.Ok(dto);
        }

        // Delegate sang PasswordHelper â€“ AuthService khÃ´ng chá»©a BCrypt logic trá»±c tiáº¿p
        // NguyÃªn táº¯c Single Responsibility: AuthService lo flow, PasswordHelper lo thuáº­t toÃ¡n
        public string HashPassword(string plainPassword) => PasswordHelper.Hash(plainPassword);
        public bool VerifyPassword(string plain, string hashed) => PasswordHelper.Verify(plain, hashed);
    }

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Auth

    /// <summary>
    /// Chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i User entity â†’ UserSessionDto.
    ///
    /// TÃ¡ch ra file riÃªng vÃ¬:
    ///   - AuthService khÃ´ng nÃªn chá»©a mapping logic (Single Responsibility)
    ///   - Dá»… tÃ¡i dÃ¹ng khi cáº§n refresh session sau nÃ y
    ///   - Dá»… unit test mapping Ä‘á»™c láº­p vá»›i logic login
    ///
    /// UserSessionDto chá»‰ chá»©a thÃ´ng tin cáº§n thiáº¿t cho UI,
    /// Ä‘áº·c biá»‡t KHÃ”NG cÃ³ PasswordHash â†’ an toÃ n hÆ¡n khi lÆ°u vÃ o AppSession.
    /// </summary>
    internal static class UserSessionMapper
    {
        internal static UserSessionDto ToDto(User user) => new()
        {
            Id         = user.Id,
            Username   = user.Username,
            FullName   = user.FullName,
            Email      = user.Email,
            AvatarPath = user.AvatarPath,
            // Láº¥y tÃªn cÃ¡c Role tá»« navigation property UserRoles â†’ Role
            // VÃ­ dá»¥ káº¿t quáº£: ["Admin"] hoáº·c ["Manager"] hoáº·c ["Developer"]
            Roles      = user.UserRoles?
                .Select(ur => ur.Role.Name)
                .ToList()
                ?? new List<string>()
        };
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Nghiá»‡p vá»¥ quáº£n lÃ½ dá»± Ã¡n: táº¡o/sá»­a/xÃ³a dá»± Ã¡n, Ä‘á»•i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i, quáº£n lÃ½ thÃ nh viÃªn.
    /// </summary>
    public class ProjectService : IProjectService
    {
        private readonly IProjectRepository _projectRepo;

        public ProjectService(IProjectRepository projectRepo)
            => _projectRepo = projectRepo;

        // Danh sÃ¡ch dá»± Ã¡n theo quyá»n
        public Task<List<Project>> GetProjectsForUserAsync(int userId, bool isManager)
            => isManager ? _projectRepo.GetAllAsync() : _projectRepo.GetByMemberAsync(userId);

        // Chi tiáº¿t Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§
        public Task<Project?> GetProjectDetailsAsync(int projectId)
            => _projectRepo.GetWithDetailsAsync(projectId);

        // Táº¡o dá»± Ã¡n má»›i
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateProjectAsync(Project project)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(project.Name))
                return (false, "TÃªn dá»± Ã¡n khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»ƒ trá»‘ng.");

            await _projectRepo.AddAsync(project);
            return (true, $"Dá»± Ã¡n \"{project.Name}\" Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c táº¡o thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        // Cáº­p nháº­t dá»± Ã¡n
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateProjectAsync(Project project)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(project.Name))
                return (false, "TÃªn dá»± Ã¡n khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»ƒ trá»‘ng.");

            await _projectRepo.UpdateAsync(project);
            return (true, "Cáº­p nháº­t dá»± Ã¡n thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        // XÃ³a dá»± Ã¡n â€“ kiá»ƒm tra cÃ³ task chÆ°a
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteProjectAsync(int projectId)
        {
            if (await _projectRepo.HasTasksAsync(projectId))
                return (false, "KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ xÃ³a dá»± Ã¡n Ä‘Ã£ cÃ³ cÃ´ng viá»‡c. HÃ£y xÃ³a cÃ´ng viá»‡c trÆ°á»›c hoáº·c chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i Cancelled.");

            await _projectRepo.DeleteAsync(projectId);
            return (true, "XÃ³a dá»± Ã¡n thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        // Äá»•i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i dá»± Ã¡n
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangeStatusAsync(int projectId, string newStatus)
        {
            var validStatuses = new[] { "NotStarted", "InProgress", "OnHold", "Completed", "Cancelled" };
            if (!validStatuses.Contains(newStatus))
                return (false, $"Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i \"{newStatus}\" khÃ´ng há»£p lá»‡.");

            await _projectRepo.UpdateStatusAsync(projectId, newStatus);
            return (true, $"ÄÃ£ chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i thÃ nh {newStatus}.");
        }

        // â”€â”€ Quáº£n lÃ½ thÃ nh viÃªn â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        public Task<List<ProjectMember>> GetMembersAsync(int projectId)
            => _projectRepo.GetMembersAsync(projectId);

        // ThÃªm thÃ nh viÃªn â€“ kiá»ƒm tra trÃ¹ng
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AddMemberAsync(
            int projectId, int userId, string projectRole)
        {
            // Kiá»ƒm tra Ä‘Ã£ lÃ  thÃ nh viÃªn chÆ°a
            var members = await _projectRepo.GetMembersAsync(projectId);
            if (members.Any(m => m.UserId == userId))
                return (false, "NgÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng Ä‘Ã£ lÃ  thÃ nh viÃªn cá»§a dá»± Ã¡n nÃ y.");

            var member = new ProjectMember
            {
                ProjectId   = projectId,
                UserId      = userId,
                ProjectRole = projectRole,
                JoinedAt    = DateTime.UtcNow
            };
            await _projectRepo.AddMemberAsync(member);
            return (true, "ThÃªm thÃ nh viÃªn thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        // XÃ³a thÃ nh viÃªn (soft delete: set LeftAt)
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> RemoveMemberAsync(int projectId, int userId)
        {
            await _projectRepo.RemoveMemberAsync(projectId, userId);
            return (true, "ÄÃ£ xÃ³a thÃ nh viÃªn khá»i dá»± Ã¡n.");
        }
    }

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Tasks
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Triá»ƒn khai ITaskService cho GD4.
    ///
    /// THá»°C Táº¾ SEED DATA (LookupSeeder.cs â€” thá»© tá»± insert = Id):
    ///   Roles:      Id=1 "Admin" | Id=2 "Manager" | Id=3 "Developer"
    ///   Statuses:   Id=1 "CREATED" | Id=2 "ASSIGNED" | Id=3 "IN-PROGRESS" | Id=4 "FAILED"
    ///               Id=5 "REVIEW-1" | Id=6 "REVIEW-2" | Id=7 "APPROVED" | Id=8 "IN-TEST"
    ///               Id=9 "RESOLVED" | Id=10 "CLOSED"
    ///   Priorities: Id=1 "Low" | Id=2 "Medium" | Id=3 "High" | Id=4 "Critical"
    ///
    /// PHÃ‚N QUYá»€N UpdateStatusAsync:
    ///   Admin / Manager â†’ bá» qua workflow, Ä‘á»•i sang Báº¤T Ká»² status nÃ o
    ///   Developer       â†’ chá»‰ Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»•i task Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao cho mÃ¬nh (AssignedToId == UserId)
    ///
    /// SO SÃNH ROLE: dÃ¹ng OrdinalIgnoreCase Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh lá»—i casing
    ///   DB seed: "Admin", "Manager", "Developer" (hoa chá»¯ cÃ¡i Ä‘áº§u)
    ///   AppSession.Roles cÃ³ thá»ƒ chá»©a báº¥t ká»³ casing nÃ o â†’ luÃ´n dÃ¹ng IgnoreCase
    /// </summary>
    public class TaskService : ITaskService
    {
        private readonly ITaskRepository _taskRepo;

        public TaskService(ITaskRepository taskRepo) => _taskRepo = taskRepo;

        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
        // TRUY Váº¤N â€” giá»¯ nguyÃªn 100%
        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

        public Task<TaskItem?> GetByIdAsync(int taskId)
            => _taskRepo.GetByIdWithDetailsAsync(taskId);

        public Task<(List<TaskItem> Items, int TotalCount)> GetPagedAsync(
            int page, int pageSize,
            int? projectId = null, int? assignedToId = null,
            int? statusId  = null, int? priorityId   = null,
            int? categoryId = null, string? keyword   = null)
            => _taskRepo.GetPagedAsync(page, pageSize,
                projectId, assignedToId, statusId, priorityId, categoryId, keyword);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetMyTasksAsync(int userId)
            => _taskRepo.GetAssignedToUserAsync(userId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForReviewer1Async(int reviewerId)
            => _taskRepo.GetByReviewer1Async(reviewerId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForReviewer2Async(int reviewerId)
            => _taskRepo.GetByReviewer2Async(reviewerId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForTesterAsync(int testerId)
            => _taskRepo.GetByTesterAsync(testerId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetOverdueTasksAsync()
            => _taskRepo.GetOverdueAsync();

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetDueSoonTasksAsync(int days = 7)
            => _taskRepo.GetDueSoonAsync(days);

        public Task<Dictionary<string, int>> GetStatusSummaryAsync(int projectId)
            => _taskRepo.GetStatusSummaryByProjectAsync(projectId);

        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
        // CRUD
        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateTaskAsync(TaskItem task)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(task.Title))
                return (false, "TiÃªu Ä‘á» cÃ´ng viá»‡c khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»ƒ trá»‘ng.");
            if (task.Title.Length > 200)
                return (false, "TiÃªu Ä‘á» khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c vÆ°á»£t quÃ¡ 200 kÃ½ tá»±.");
            if (task.ProjectId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃ²ng chá»n dá»± Ã¡n cho cÃ´ng viá»‡c.");
            if (task.PriorityId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃ²ng chá»n má»©c Ä‘á»™ Æ°u tiÃªn.");
            if (task.StatusId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃ²ng chá»n tráº¡ng thÃ¡i.");
            if (task.CategoryId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃ²ng chá»n loáº¡i cÃ´ng viá»‡c.");
            if (task.EstimatedHours.HasValue && task.EstimatedHours.Value <= 0)
                return (false, "Sá»‘ giá» Æ°á»›c tÃ­nh pháº£i lá»›n hÆ¡n 0.");
            if (task.DueDate.HasValue && task.DueDate.Value < DateTime.UtcNow.AddDays(-1))
                return (false, "Háº¡n chÃ³t khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c lÃ  ngÃ y trong quÃ¡ khá»©.");

            task.Title       = task.Title.Trim();
            task.Description = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(task.Description)
                ? null : task.Description.Trim();

            await _taskRepo.AddAsync(task);
            return (true, $"ÄÃ£ táº¡o cÃ´ng viá»‡c \"{task.Title}\" thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Cáº­p nháº­t task â€” gá»i 2 method Repository riÃªng biá»‡t Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh EF tracking conflict:
        ///
        ///   1. UpdateAsync(task)
        ///      DÃ¹ng Attach + State.Modified Ä‘á»ƒ cáº­p nháº­t cÃ¡c trÆ°á»ng ná»™i dung
        ///      (Title, Description, AssignedToId, PriorityId, DueDate, v.v.)
        ///      Tuy nhiÃªn khi entity load báº±ng AsNoTracking cÃ³ navigation property
        ///      (task.Status, task.Priority lÃ  object), EF Ä‘Ã´i khi khÃ´ng ghi FK Ä‘Ãºng.
        ///
        ///   2. UpdateStatusAsync(task.Id, task.StatusId)
        ///      DÃ¹ng ExecuteUpdateAsync â€” sinh SQL "SET StatusId=? WHERE Id=?" trá»±c tiáº¿p,
        ///      khÃ´ng phá»¥ thuá»™c vÃ o tracking state â†’ Ä‘áº£m báº£o StatusId luÃ´n Ä‘Æ°á»£c ghi Ä‘Ãºng.
        ///
        /// TÆ°Æ¡ng tá»±: AssignedToId cÅ©ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c UpdateAsync ghi Ä‘Ãºng vÃ¬ lÃ  FK thuáº§n (int?),
        /// khÃ´ng cÃ³ navigation conflict phá»©c táº¡p nhÆ° StatusId.
        /// </summary>
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateTaskAsync(TaskItem task)
        {
            // 1. Validation cÆ¡ báº£n
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(task.Title))
                return (false, "TiÃªu Ä‘á» cÃ´ng viá»‡c khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»ƒ trá»‘ng.");

            try
            {
                // 2. LÃ m sáº¡ch dá»¯ liá»‡u
                task.Title = task.Title.Trim();
                task.Description = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(task.Description) ? null : task.Description.Trim();

                // 3. Cáº¬P NHáº¬T Tá»”NG THá»‚ (Quan trá»ng)
                // Thay vÃ¬ gá»i 2 hÃ m tÃ¡ch biá»‡t, hÃ£y dÃ¹ng UpdateAsync Ä‘á»ƒ EF tá»± quáº£n lÃ½ 
                // hoáº·c kiá»ƒm tra láº¡i hÃ m UpdateStatusAsync trong Repository cá»§a báº¡n.

                await _taskRepo.UpdateAsync(task);

                // Äáº£m báº£o StatusId Ä‘Æ°á»£c cáº­p nháº­t cuá»‘i cÃ¹ng náº¿u UpdateAsync gáº·p váº¥n Ä‘á» vá»›i Navigation Property
                await _taskRepo.UpdateStatusAsync(task.Id, task.StatusId);

                return (true, "Cáº­p nháº­t cÃ´ng viá»‡c thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return (false, "Lá»—i khi lÆ°u vÃ o Database: " + ex.Message);
            }
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteTaskAsync(int taskId)
        {
            var task = await _taskRepo.GetByIdWithDetailsAsync(taskId);
            if (task == null)
                return (false, "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y cÃ´ng viá»‡c.");
            if (task.SubTasks.Count > 0)
                return (false,
                    $"KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ xÃ³a vÃ¬ cÃ´ng viá»‡c nÃ y cÃ³ {task.SubTasks.Count} cÃ´ng viá»‡c con. " +
                    "HÃ£y xÃ³a cÃ¡c cÃ´ng viá»‡c con trÆ°á»›c.");

            await _taskRepo.DeleteAsync(taskId);
            return (true, $"ÄÃ£ xÃ³a cÃ´ng viá»‡c \"{task.Title}\".");
        }

        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
        // Cáº¬P NHáº¬T TIáº¾N Äá»˜
        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateProgressAsync(
            int taskId, byte progress)
        {
            if (progress > 100)
                return (false, "Tiáº¿n Ä‘á»™ pháº£i tá»« 0 Ä‘áº¿n 100.");

            // Lookup Id cá»§a RESOLVED tá»« DB â€” khÃ´ng hard-code
            // Theo seed: RESOLVED = DisplayOrder 8, thá»© 9 trong list â†’ Id=9
            var statuses       = await _taskRepo.GetAllStatusesAsync();
            var resolvedStatus = statuses.FirstOrDefault(
                s => s.Name.Equals("RESOLVED", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

            if (resolvedStatus == null)
                return (false, "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y tráº¡ng thÃ¡i RESOLVED trong há»‡ thá»‘ng.");

            await _taskRepo.UpdateProgressAsync(taskId, progress, resolvedStatus.Id);

            return progress == 100
                ? (true, "ðŸŽ‰ CÃ´ng viá»‡c Ä‘Ã£ hoÃ n thÃ nh! Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i chuyá»ƒn sang RESOLVED.")
                : (true, $"ÄÃ£ cáº­p nháº­t tiáº¿n Ä‘á»™ {progress}%.");
        }

        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
        // Cáº¬P NHáº¬T TRáº NG THÃI â€” PHÃ‚N QUYá»€N LINH HOáº T
        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

        /// <summary>
        /// Chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i workflow vá»›i phÃ¢n quyá»n linh hoáº¡t.
        ///
        /// PHÃ‚N QUYá»€N:
        ///   Admin / Manager â†’ Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»•i sang Báº¤T Ká»² trong 10 status, bá» qua workflow.
        ///   Developer       â†’ chá»‰ Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»•i task Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao cho mÃ¬nh (AssignedToId == UserId).
        ///
        /// THAM Sá» statusId:
        ///   Truyá»n Id trá»±c tiáº¿p tá»« ComboBox (KHÃ”NG dÃ¹ng tÃªn string) Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh lá»—i
        ///   so khá»›p tÃªn khi DB seed hoáº·c casing thay Ä‘á»•i.
        ///
        /// SO SÃNH ROLE (quan trá»ng):
        ///   DB seed: "Admin", "Manager", "Developer"
        ///   AppSession.Roles: List&lt;string&gt; â€” dÃ¹ng OrdinalIgnoreCase Ä‘á»ƒ khÃ´ng lá»—i
        ///   náº¿u source nÃ o Ä‘Ã³ tráº£ vá» "admin", "MANAGER", "developer"...
        /// </summary>
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateStatusAsync(
            int           taskId,
            int           statusId,
            int           requesterId,
            IList<string> requesterRoles)
        {
            // â”€â”€ Validate statusId â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            if (statusId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃ²ng chá»n tráº¡ng thÃ¡i há»£p lá»‡.");

            var statuses = await _taskRepo.GetAllStatusesAsync();
            var target   = statuses.FirstOrDefault(s => s.Id == statusId);
            if (target == null)
                return (false, $"Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i khÃ´ng tá»“n táº¡i (Id={statusId}).");

            // â”€â”€ Admin/Manager: bá» qua má»i kiá»ƒm tra â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            // So sÃ¡nh OrdinalIgnoreCase: "Admin"/"admin"/"ADMIN" Ä‘á»u match
            bool isManagerOrAbove =
                requesterRoles.Any(r => r.Equals("Admin",   StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) ||
                requesterRoles.Any(r => r.Equals("Manager", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

            if (isManagerOrAbove)
            {
                // ExecuteUpdateAsync: SET StatusId=? WHERE Id=? â€” khÃ´ng cáº§n load entity
                await _taskRepo.UpdateStatusAsync(taskId, statusId);
                return (true, $"ÄÃ£ chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i sang \"{target.Name}\".");
            }

            // â”€â”€ Developer: pháº£i load task Ä‘á»ƒ kiá»ƒm tra quyá»n â”€
            var task = await _taskRepo.GetByIdAsync(taskId);
            if (task == null)
                return (false, "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y cÃ´ng viá»‡c.");

            bool isAssignee = task.AssignedToId.HasValue
                           && task.AssignedToId.Value == requesterId;

            if (!isAssignee)
                return (false,
                    "Báº¡n chá»‰ cÃ³ thá»ƒ thay Ä‘á»•i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i cÃ´ng viá»‡c Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao cho mÃ¬nh.\n" +
                    "LiÃªn há»‡ Manager náº¿u cáº§n thay Ä‘á»•i task khÃ¡c.");

            await _taskRepo.UpdateStatusAsync(taskId, statusId);
            return (true, $"ÄÃ£ chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i sang \"{target.Name}\".");
        }

        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
        // ASSIGN & TRANSITION
        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AssignAndTransitionAsync(
            int taskId, string newStatus,
            int? reviewer1Id = null, int? reviewer2Id = null, int? testerId = null)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(newStatus))
                return (false, "TÃªn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»ƒ trá»‘ng.");

            var statuses = await _taskRepo.GetAllStatusesAsync();
            // OrdinalIgnoreCase cho AssignAndTransition vÃ¬ caller truyá»n tÃªn string
            var target   = statuses.FirstOrDefault(
                s => s.Name.Equals(newStatus, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

            if (target == null)
                return (false, $"Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i \"{newStatus}\" khÃ´ng há»£p lá»‡.");

            var task = await _taskRepo.GetByIdAsync(taskId);
            if (task == null)
                return (false, "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y cÃ´ng viá»‡c.");

            if (reviewer1Id.HasValue && reviewer1Id.Value <= 0)
                return (false, "Reviewer láº§n 1 khÃ´ng há»£p lá»‡.");
            if (reviewer2Id.HasValue && reviewer2Id.Value <= 0)
                return (false, "Reviewer láº§n 2 khÃ´ng há»£p lá»‡.");
            if (testerId.HasValue && testerId.Value <= 0)
                return (false, "Tester khÃ´ng há»£p lá»‡.");

            await _taskRepo.AssignReviewerAsync(
                taskId, reviewer1Id, reviewer2Id, testerId, target.Id);

            var parts = new List<string>();
            if (reviewer1Id.HasValue) parts.Add("Reviewer 1");
            if (reviewer2Id.HasValue) parts.Add("Reviewer 2");
            if (testerId.HasValue)    parts.Add("Tester");

            var extra = parts.Count > 0 ? $" â€” Ä‘Ã£ gÃ¡n {string.Join(", ", parts)}" : string.Empty;
            return (true, $"Chuyá»ƒn sang {newStatus}{extra} thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
        // LOOKUP
        // â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

        public Task<List<Status>>   GetAllStatusesAsync()   => _taskRepo.GetAllStatusesAsync();
        public Task<List<Priority>> GetAllPrioritiesAsync() => _taskRepo.GetAllPrioritiesAsync();
        public Task<List<Category>> GetAllCategoriesAsync() => _taskRepo.GetAllCategoriesAsync();
    }
}
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Users
{
    public class UserService : IUserService
    {
        private readonly IUserRepository _userRepo;
        private readonly IAuthService    _authService;

        public UserService(IUserRepository userRepo, IAuthService authService)
        {
            _userRepo    = userRepo;
            _authService = authService;
        }

        public Task<List<User>> GetAllUsersAsync()        => _userRepo.GetAllWithRolesAsync();
        public Task<List<User>> GetAllActiveUsersAsync()  => _userRepo.GetAllAsync();
        public Task<User?> GetByIdAsync(int id)           => _userRepo.GetByIdAsync(id);

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateUserAsync(
            string username, string fullName, string email, string password, string roleName, string? phone = null)
        {
            if (!ValidationHelper.IsValidUsername(username))
                return (false, "Username chá»‰ gá»“m chá»¯, sá»‘, dáº¥u gáº¡ch dÆ°á»›i (3â€“50 kÃ½ tá»±).");
            if (await _userRepo.IsUsernameExistsAsync(username))
                return (false, $"Username '{username}' Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i.");
            if (!ValidationHelper.IsValidEmail(email))
                return (false, "Email khÃ´ng há»£p lá»‡.");
            if (!ValidationHelper.IsPasswordStrong(password))
                return (false, "Máº­t kháº©u pháº£i cÃ³ Ã­t nháº¥t 6 kÃ½ tá»±.");

            var user = new User
            {
                Username     = username.Trim(),
                FullName     = fullName.Trim(),
                Email        = email.Trim(),
                Phone        = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(phone) ? null : phone.Trim(),
                PasswordHash = _authService.HashPassword(password),
                IsActive     = true
            };
            await _userRepo.AddWithRoleAsync(user, roleName);
            return (true, $"Táº¡o tÃ i khoáº£n '{username}' thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateUserAsync(User user)
        {
            await _userRepo.UpdateAsync(user);
            return (true, "Cáº­p nháº­t thÃ´ng tin thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeactivateUserAsync(int userId)
        {
            await _userRepo.SetActiveAsync(userId, false);
            return (true, "TÃ i khoáº£n Ä‘Ã£ bá»‹ vÃ´ hiá»‡u hÃ³a.");
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ActivateUserAsync(int userId)
        {
            await _userRepo.SetActiveAsync(userId, true);
            return (true, "TÃ i khoáº£n Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c kÃ­ch hoáº¡t láº¡i.");
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangePasswordAsync(
            int userId, string oldPassword, string newPassword)
        {
            var user = await _userRepo.GetByIdAsync(userId);
            if (user == null)
                return (false, "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y tÃ i khoáº£n.");
            if (!_authService.VerifyPassword(oldPassword, user.PasswordHash))
                return (false, "Máº­t kháº©u cÅ© khÃ´ng Ä‘Ãºng.");
            if (!ValidationHelper.IsPasswordStrong(newPassword))
                return (false, "Máº­t kháº©u má»›i pháº£i cÃ³ Ã­t nháº¥t 6 kÃ½ tá»±.");

            await _userRepo.UpdatePasswordAsync(userId, _authService.HashPassword(newPassword));
            return (true, "Äá»•i máº­t kháº©u thÃ nh cÃ´ng.");
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Äá»•i vai trÃ² cho user (chá»‰ Admin gá»i tá»« form).
        /// XÃ³a táº¥t cáº£ role cÅ© â†’ gÃ¡n role má»›i.
        /// </summary>
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangeRoleAsync(int userId, string newRoleName)
        {
            try
            {
                await _userRepo.ChangeRoleAsync(userId, newRoleName);
                return (true, $"ÄÃ£ Ä‘á»•i vai trÃ² thÃ nh {newRoleName}.");
            }
            catch (InvalidOperationException ex)
            {
                return (false, ex.Message);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return (false, "Lá»—i khi Ä‘á»•i vai trÃ²: " + (ex.InnerException?.Message ?? ex.Message));
            }
        }
    }
}
using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Design;
using TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure
{
    public class DesignTimeDbContextFactory
        : IDesignTimeDbContextFactory<AppDbContext>
    {
        public AppDbContext CreateDbContext(string[] args)
        {
            var optionsBuilder = new DbContextOptionsBuilder<AppDbContext>();

            optionsBuilder.UseSqlServer(
                "Server=.\\SQLEXPRESS2022;Database=TaskFlowManagementDb;Trusted_Connection=True;TrustServerCertificate=True;"
            );

            return new AppDbContext(optionsBuilder.Options);
        }
    }
}
using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data
{
    /// <summary>
    /// AppDbContext â€“ cáº§u ná»‘i giá»¯a C# entities vÃ  SQL Server database.
    /// Cáº¥u hÃ¬nh quan há»‡ báº±ng Fluent API trong OnModelCreating.
    /// 
    /// GD3: ThÃªm relationships cho Reviewer1, Reviewer2, Tester trÃªn TaskItem.
    /// </summary>
    public class AppDbContext : DbContext
    {
        // â”€â”€ DbSets: má»—i property = 1 báº£ng trong DB â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        public DbSet<User>          Users          { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Role>          Roles          { get; set; }
        public DbSet<UserRole>      UserRoles      { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Customer>      Customers      { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Project>       Projects       { get; set; }
        public DbSet<ProjectMember> ProjectMembers { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Expense>       Expenses       { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Category>      Categories     { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Priority>      Priorities     { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Status>        Statuses       { get; set; }
        public DbSet<TaskItem>      TaskItems      { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Comment>       Comments       { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Attachment>    Attachments    { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Tag>           Tags           { get; set; }
        public DbSet<TaskTag>       TaskTags       { get; set; }

        public AppDbContext(DbContextOptions<AppDbContext> options) : base(options) { }

        protected override void OnModelCreating(ModelBuilder modelBuilder)
        {
            base.OnModelCreating(modelBuilder);

            // â”€â”€ Composite Keys â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            modelBuilder.Entity<UserRole>()
                .HasKey(ur => new { ur.UserId, ur.RoleId });

            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskTag>()
                .HasKey(tt => new { tt.TaskItemId, tt.TagId });

            // â”€â”€ User Relationships â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            modelBuilder.Entity<UserRole>()
                .HasOne(ur => ur.User).WithMany(u => u.UserRoles)
                .HasForeignKey(ur => ur.UserId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<UserRole>()
                .HasOne(ur => ur.Role).WithMany(r => r.UserRoles)
                .HasForeignKey(ur => ur.RoleId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<User>()
                .HasIndex(u => u.Email).IsUnique();
            modelBuilder.Entity<User>()
                .HasIndex(u => u.Username).IsUnique();

            // â”€â”€ Project Relationships â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>()
                .HasOne(p => p.Owner).WithMany(u => u.OwnedProjects)
                .HasForeignKey(p => p.OwnerId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>()
                .HasOne(p => p.Customer).WithMany(c => c.Projects)
                .HasForeignKey(p => p.CustomerId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.SetNull);

            modelBuilder.Entity<ProjectMember>()
                .HasOne(pm => pm.Project).WithMany(p => p.Members)
                .HasForeignKey(pm => pm.ProjectId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<ProjectMember>()
                .HasOne(pm => pm.User).WithMany(u => u.ProjectMemberships)
                .HasForeignKey(pm => pm.UserId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            modelBuilder.Entity<ProjectMember>()
                .HasIndex(pm => new { pm.ProjectId, pm.UserId }).IsUnique();

            // â”€â”€ Task Relationships â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

            // NgÆ°á»i táº¡o task
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.CreatedBy).WithMany(u => u.CreatedTasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.CreatedById)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // NgÆ°á»i Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao thá»±c hiá»‡n
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.AssignedTo).WithMany(u => u.AssignedTasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.AssignedToId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // GD3: Reviewer láº§n 1 (peer review)
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.Reviewer1).WithMany(u => u.Review1Tasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.Reviewer1Id)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // GD3: Reviewer láº§n 2 (senior review)
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.Reviewer2).WithMany(u => u.Review2Tasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.Reviewer2Id)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // GD3: Tester (QA)
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.Tester).WithMany(u => u.TesterTasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.TesterId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // Task cha â†’ Task con (self-referencing)
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.ParentTask).WithMany(t => t.SubTasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.ParentTaskId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // â”€â”€ Expense Relationships â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            modelBuilder.Entity<Expense>()
                .HasOne(e => e.Project).WithMany(p => p.Expenses)
                .HasForeignKey(e => e.ProjectId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<Expense>()
                .HasOne(e => e.CreatedBy).WithMany(u => u.CreatedExpenses)
                .HasForeignKey(e => e.CreatedById)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // â”€â”€ Attachment & Tag â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            modelBuilder.Entity<Attachment>()
                .HasOne(a => a.UploadedBy).WithMany()
                .HasForeignKey(a => a.UploadedById)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskTag>()
                .HasOne(tt => tt.TaskItem).WithMany(t => t.TaskTags)
                .HasForeignKey(tt => tt.TaskItemId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskTag>()
                .HasOne(tt => tt.Tag).WithMany(t => t.TaskTags)
                .HasForeignKey(tt => tt.TagId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            // â”€â”€ Indexes â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.ProjectId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_ProjectId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.StatusId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_StatusId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.PriorityId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_PriorityId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.AssignedToId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_AssignedToId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.DueDate).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_DueDate");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.CreatedAt).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_CreatedAt");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => new { t.ProjectId, t.StatusId }).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_ProjectId_StatusId");

            // GD3: Index cho Reviewer/Tester queries
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.Reviewer1Id).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_Reviewer1Id");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.Reviewer2Id).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_Reviewer2Id");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.TesterId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_TesterId");

            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>().HasIndex(p => p.OwnerId).HasDatabaseName("IX_Projects_OwnerId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>().HasIndex(p => p.Status).HasDatabaseName("IX_Projects_Status");
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>().HasIndex(p => p.CustomerId).HasDatabaseName("IX_Projects_CustomerId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<Comment>().HasIndex(c => c.TaskItemId).HasDatabaseName("IX_Comments_TaskItemId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<Expense>().HasIndex(e => e.ProjectId).HasDatabaseName("IX_Expenses_ProjectId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<ProjectMember>().HasIndex(pm => pm.UserId).HasDatabaseName("IX_ProjectMembers_UserId");
        }
    }
}
using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data.Seed;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Orchestrator seed data â€“ gá»i cÃ¡c Seeder nhá» theo Ä‘Ãºng thá»© tá»± FK.
    ///
    /// THá»¨ Tá»° Báº®T BUá»˜C (do Foreign Key):
    ///   1. Lookup tables (Roles, Priorities, Statuses, Categories, Tags)
    ///   2. Users
    ///   3. UserRoles (cáº§n UserId + RoleId)
    ///   4. Customers
    ///   5. Projects (cáº§n UserId + CustomerId)
    ///   6. ProjectMembers (cáº§n ProjectId + UserId)
    ///   7. TaskItems (cáº§n ProjectId + UserId + StatusId + PriorityId + CategoryId)
    ///
    /// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    /// âš ï¸  KHI NÃ€O Cáº¦N RESET DATABASE?
    ///
    ///   Náº¿u trÆ°á»›c Ä‘Ã¢y cháº¡y version dÃ¹ng SHA-256 (hash cÅ©),
    ///   DB Ä‘ang cÃ³ hash sai format â†’ login sáº½ bÃ¡o sai máº­t kháº©u.
    ///
    ///   CÃCH RESET (chá»n 1 trong 3):
    ///
    ///   [A] SQL Server Management Studio (SSMS):
    ///       Káº¿t ná»‘i â†’ chuá»™t pháº£i TaskFlowManagementDb â†’ Delete â†’ OK
    ///
    ///   [B] Package Manager Console (Visual Studio):
    ///       Tools â†’ NuGet Package Manager â†’ Package Manager Console
    ///       Chá»n Default project: TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure
    ///       GÃµ lá»‡nh:
    ///           Drop-Database
    ///       XÃ¡c nháº­n Y â†’ Enter
    ///
    ///   [C] Terminal / CMD:
    ///       cd TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure
    ///       dotnet ef database drop --force
    ///
    ///   Sau khi drop â†’ cháº¡y láº¡i app â†’ DB tá»± táº¡o má»›i + seed BCrypt.
    /// â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
    /// </summary>
    public static class DbSeeder
    {
        public static async Task SeedAsync(AppDbContext context)
        {
            // Guard: chá»‰ seed khi DB hoÃ n toÃ n trá»‘ng
            // Náº¿u Ä‘Ã£ cÃ³ user â†’ bá» qua toÃ n bá»™ (idempotent)
            if (await context.Users.AnyAsync()) return;

            // =====================================================
            // BÆ¯á»šC 1: LOOKUP TABLES
            // Pháº£i commit trÆ°á»›c Ä‘á»ƒ cÃ³ ID cho cÃ¡c báº£ng phá»¥ thuá»™c
            // =====================================================
            var roles      = LookupSeeder.GetRoles();
            var priorities = LookupSeeder.GetPriorities();
            var statuses   = LookupSeeder.GetStatuses();
            var categories = LookupSeeder.GetCategories();
            var tags       = LookupSeeder.GetTags();

            context.AddRange(roles);
            context.AddRange(priorities);
            context.AddRange(statuses);
            context.AddRange(categories);
            context.AddRange(tags);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();
            // Sau SaveChanges: roles[0].Id, priorities[0].Id, ... Ä‘Ã£ cÃ³ giÃ¡ trá»‹ tá»« DB

            // =====================================================
            // BÆ¯á»šC 2: USERS (password hash báº±ng BCrypt â€“ xem SeedHelper)
            // =====================================================
            var users = UserSeeder.GetUsers();
            context.AddRange(users);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();
            // Sau Ä‘Ã¢y users[i].Id Ä‘Ã£ cÃ³ giÃ¡ trá»‹

            // =====================================================
            // BÆ¯á»šC 3: USER ROLES â€“ gÃ¡n quyá»n theo username pattern
            // =====================================================
            var adminRole   = roles.First(r => r.Name == "Admin");
            var managerRole = roles.First(r => r.Name == "Manager");
            var devRole     = roles.First(r => r.Name == "Developer");

            var userRoles = users.Select(u => new UserRole
            {
                UserId = u.Id,
                RoleId = u.Username switch
                {
                    "admin"                              => adminRole.Id,
                    var n when n.StartsWith("manager")  => managerRole.Id,
                    _                                   => devRole.Id
                }
            }).ToList();

            context.AddRange(userRoles);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();

            // =====================================================
            // BÆ¯á»šC 4: CUSTOMERS + PROJECTS
            // =====================================================
            var customers = ProjectSeeder.GetCustomers();
            context.AddRange(customers);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();

            var projects = ProjectSeeder.GetProjects(users, customers);
            context.AddRange(projects);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();

            // =====================================================
            // BÆ¯á»šC 5: PROJECT MEMBERS â€“ má»—i project 3-5 devs ngáº«u nhiÃªn
            // =====================================================
            var devUsers = users.Where(u => u.Username.StartsWith("dev")).ToList();
            var rng      = new Random(42); // seed cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh â†’ reproducible

            var members = new List<ProjectMember>();
            foreach (var project in projects)
            {
                var assigned = devUsers
                    .OrderBy(_ => rng.Next())
                    .Take(rng.Next(3, 6))
                    .ToList();

                members.AddRange(assigned.Select(dev => new ProjectMember
                {
                    ProjectId   = project.Id,
                    UserId      = dev.Id,
                    ProjectRole = "Developer",
                    JoinedAt    = project.CreatedAt
                }));
            }
            context.AddRange(members);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();

            // =====================================================
            // BÆ¯á»šC 6: TASK ITEMS â€“ 10 task máº«u má»—i project
            // =====================================================
            var taskList = BuildTaskItems(
                projects, members, users, priorities, statuses, categories, rng);

            context.AddRange(taskList);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();
        }

        // -------------------------------------------------------
        // TÃ¡ch logic táº¡o task ra method riÃªng cho gá»n
        // -------------------------------------------------------
        private static List<TaskItem> BuildTaskItems(
            List<Project>       projects,
            List<ProjectMember> members,
            List<User>          users,
            List<Priority>      priorities,
            List<Status>        statuses,
            List<Category>      categories,
            Random              rng)
        {
            var now = DateTime.UtcNow;

            // Template (title, category, priority)
            var templates = new[]
            {
                ("PhÃ¢n tÃ­ch yÃªu cáº§u há»‡ thá»‘ng",     "Feature",     "High"),
                ("Thiáº¿t káº¿ database schema",         "Feature",     "High"),
                ("CÃ i Ä‘áº·t mÃ´i trÆ°á»ng development",   "Feature",     "Medium"),
                ("XÃ¢y dá»±ng module xÃ¡c thá»±c Login",   "Feature",     "Critical"),
                ("API quáº£n lÃ½ ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng",           "Feature",     "High"),
                ("UI Dashboard tá»•ng quan",           "Feature",     "Medium"),
                ("Fix bug phÃ¢n quyá»n sai",           "Bug",         "High"),
                ("Viáº¿t unit test Auth module",       "Testing",     "Medium"),
                ("Tá»‘i Æ°u query performance",         "Improvement", "Medium"),
                ("Review code Pull Request #12",     "Research",    "Low"),
            };

            var result = new List<TaskItem>();

            foreach (var project in projects)
            {
                var projectDevs = members
                    .Where(m => m.ProjectId == project.Id)
                    .Select(m => users.First(u => u.Id == m.UserId))
                    .ToList();

                var owner = users.First(u => u.Id == project.OwnerId);

                for (int i = 0; i < templates.Length; i++)
                {
                    var (title, catName, priName) = templates[i];
                    var priority = priorities.First(p => p.Name == priName);
                    var status   = statuses[rng.Next(statuses.Count)];
                    var category = categories.FirstOrDefault(c => c.Name == catName)
                                   ?? categories.First();
                    var assignee = projectDevs.Count > 0
                        ? projectDevs[i % projectDevs.Count]
                        : owner;

                    var progress = status.Name == "Done"       ? (byte)100
                                 : status.Name == "InProgress" ? (byte)rng.Next(20, 80)
                                 : (byte)0;

                    result.Add(new TaskItem
                    {
                        Title           = title,
                        Description     = $"[{project.Name}] {title}",
                        ProjectId       = project.Id,
                        CreatedById     = owner.Id,
                        AssignedToId    = assignee.Id,
                        PriorityId      = priority.Id,
                        StatusId        = status.Id,
                        CategoryId      = category.Id,
                        DueDate         = now.AddDays(rng.Next(-7, 30)),
                        ProgressPercent = progress,
                        IsCompleted     = progress == 100,
                        EstimatedHours  = rng.Next(2, 20),
                        CreatedAt       = project.CreatedAt.AddDays(rng.Next(0, 10)),
                        UpdatedAt       = now,
                        CompletedAt     = progress == 100
                                          ? now.AddDays(-rng.Next(1, 7))
                                          : null
                    });
                }
            }

            return result;
        }
    }
}
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data.Seed
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Seed dá»¯ liá»‡u cho cÃ¡c báº£ng Lookup: Roles, Priorities, Statuses, Categories, Tags.
    /// 
    /// âš ï¸ GD3: Statuses Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c thay Ä‘á»•i tá»« 4 â†’ 10 tráº¡ng thÃ¡i.
    ///    Náº¿u DB cÅ© cÃ²n 4 status â†’ cáº§n DROP DB rá»“i cháº¡y láº¡i Ä‘á»ƒ seed má»›i.
    /// </summary>
    internal static class LookupSeeder
    {
        internal static List<Role> GetRoles() => new()
        {
            new() { Name = "Admin",     Description = "ToÃ n quyá»n há»‡ thá»‘ng" },
            new() { Name = "Manager",   Description = "Quáº£n lÃ½ dá»± Ã¡n, khÃ¡ch hÃ ng, bÃ¡o cÃ¡o" },
            new() { Name = "Developer", Description = "Thá»±c hiá»‡n cÃ´ng viá»‡c Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao" }
        };

        internal static List<Priority> GetPriorities() => new()
        {
            new() { Name = "Low",      Level = 1, ColorHex = "#4CAF50" },
            new() { Name = "Medium",   Level = 2, ColorHex = "#FF9800" },
            new() { Name = "High",     Level = 3, ColorHex = "#F44336" },
            new() { Name = "Critical", Level = 4, ColorHex = "#9C27B0" }
        };

        /// <summary>
        /// 10 tráº¡ng thÃ¡i workflow quáº£n lÃ½ dá»± Ã¡n pháº§n má»m:
        /// 
        /// Luá»“ng chÃ­nh:
        ///   CREATED â†’ ASSIGNED â†’ IN-PROGRESS â†’ REVIEW-1 â†’ REVIEW-2 â†’ APPROVED â†’ IN-TEST â†’ RESOLVED â†’ CLOSED
        /// 
        /// Luá»“ng reject (khi khÃ´ng Ä‘áº¡t yÃªu cáº§u):
        ///   REVIEW-1 / REVIEW-2 / IN-TEST â†’ FAILED â†’ IN-PROGRESS
        /// 
        /// Ai chuyá»ƒn tráº¡ng thÃ¡i:
        ///   CREATED â†’ ASSIGNED:      Manager táº¡o vÃ  giao task
        ///   ASSIGNED â†’ IN-PROGRESS:  Developer báº¯t Ä‘áº§u lÃ m
        ///   IN-PROGRESS â†’ REVIEW-1:  Developer xong, gÃ¡n Reviewer1
        ///   REVIEW-1 â†’ REVIEW-2:     Reviewer1 approve, gÃ¡n Reviewer2
        ///   REVIEW-1 â†’ FAILED:       Reviewer1 reject
        ///   REVIEW-2 â†’ APPROVED:     Reviewer2 approve
        ///   REVIEW-2 â†’ FAILED:       Reviewer2 reject
        ///   APPROVED â†’ IN-TEST:      Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng hoáº·c Manager gÃ¡n Tester
        ///   IN-TEST â†’ RESOLVED:      Tester pass
        ///   IN-TEST â†’ FAILED:        Tester reject
        ///   RESOLVED â†’ CLOSED:       Manager xÃ¡c nháº­n Ä‘Ã³ng task
        ///   FAILED â†’ IN-PROGRESS:    Developer sá»­a láº¡i vÃ  lÃ m tiáº¿p
        /// </summary>
        internal static List<Status> GetStatuses() => new()
        {
            new() { Name = "CREATED",     DisplayOrder = 0,  ColorHex = "#9E9E9E",
                     Description = "Task vá»«a Ä‘Æ°á»£c táº¡o, chá» phÃ¢n cÃ´ng vÃ  review yÃªu cáº§u" },
            new() { Name = "ASSIGNED",    DisplayOrder = 1,  ColorHex = "#607D8B",
                     Description = "ÄÃ£ giao cho developer, sáºµn sÃ ng thá»±c hiá»‡n" },
            new() { Name = "IN-PROGRESS", DisplayOrder = 2,  ColorHex = "#2196F3",
                     Description = "Developer Ä‘ang thá»±c hiá»‡n code" },
            new() { Name = "FAILED",      DisplayOrder = 3,  ColorHex = "#F44336",
                     Description = "Bá»‹ reject tá»« review hoáº·c test, cáº§n sá»­a láº¡i" },
            new() { Name = "REVIEW-1",    DisplayOrder = 4,  ColorHex = "#FF9800",
                     Description = "Chá» review láº§n 1 tá»« peer hoáº·c team lead" },
            new() { Name = "REVIEW-2",    DisplayOrder = 5,  ColorHex = "#FF5722",

using BCrypt.Net;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data.Seed
{
    /// <summary>
    /// HÃ m tiá»‡n Ã­ch dÃ¹ng chung cho toÃ n bá»™ Seeder.
    /// TÃ¡ch riÃªng Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh láº·p code vÃ  dá»… thay Ä‘á»•i thuáº­t toÃ¡n hash sau nÃ y.
    /// </summary>
    internal static class SeedHelper
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Hash máº­t kháº©u báº±ng BCrypt WorkFactor 12.
        ///
        /// âš ï¸ FIX: PhiÃªn báº£n cÅ© dÃ¹ng SHA-256 + Salt tÄ©nh.
        /// PhiÃªn báº£n nÃ y Ä‘Ã£ chuyá»ƒn sang BCrypt â€“ salt tá»± Ä‘á»™ng, khÃ¡c nhau má»—i láº§n hash.
        ///
        /// Náº¾U Báº N ÄÃƒ Tá»ªNG CHáº Y VERSION CÅ¨ (SHA-256):
        ///   Pháº£i xÃ³a DB cÅ© trÆ°á»›c: DROP DATABASE TaskFlowManagementDb
        ///   Sau Ä‘Ã³ cháº¡y láº¡i app Ä‘á»ƒ seed báº±ng BCrypt.
        /// </summary>
        internal static string Hash(string password)
            => BCrypt.Net.BCrypt.HashPassword(password, workFactor: 12);
    }
}

        public async Task<List<Customer>> SearchAsync(string keyword)
        {

                .OrderBy(c => c.CompanyName)
