        // PAINT EVENTS â€“ khai bÃ¡o riÃªng ngoÃ i InitializeComponent
        // Designer chá»‰ cáº§n tháº¥y tÃªn method, khÃ´ng tháº¥y logic bÃªn trong
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        // Váº½ vÃ²ng trÃ²n ring 1 (mÃ u xanh navy nháº¡t)
        private void panelRing1_Paint(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.PaintEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Graphics.SmoothingMode = System.Drawing.Drawing2D.SmoothingMode.AntiAlias;
            using var pen = new System.Drawing.Pen(System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(30, 37, 99, 235), 1f);
            e.Graphics.DrawEllipse(pen, 0, 0, panelRing1.Width - 1, panelRing1.Height - 1);
        }

        // Váº½ vÃ²ng trÃ²n ring 2 (mÃ u teal nháº¡t)
        private void panelRing2_Paint(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.PaintEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Graphics.SmoothingMode = System.Drawing.Drawing2D.SmoothingMode.AntiAlias;
            using var pen = new System.Drawing.Pen(System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(25, 6, 182, 212), 1f);
            e.Graphics.DrawEllipse(pen, 0, 0, panelRing2.Width - 1, panelRing2.Height - 1);
        }

        // Váº½ logo box: ná»n gradient xanh + bo gÃ³c 12px
        private void panelLogoBox_Paint(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.PaintEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Graphics.SmoothingMode = System.Drawing.Drawing2D.SmoothingMode.AntiAlias;
            var rect = new System.Drawing.Rectangle(0, 0, panelLogoBox.Width, panelLogoBox.Height);
            using var brush = new System.Drawing.Drawing2D.LinearGradientBrush(
                rect,
                System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(37, 99, 235),
                System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(6, 182, 212),
                135f);
            using var path = CreateRoundedPath(rect, 12);
            e.Graphics.FillPath(brush, path);
        }

        // Váº½ badge pill: viá»n bo gÃ³c mÃ u xanh nháº¡t
        private void panelBadge_Paint(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.PaintEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Graphics.SmoothingMode = System.Drawing.Drawing2D.SmoothingMode.AntiAlias;
            var rect = new System.Drawing.Rectangle(0, 0, panelBadge.Width - 1, panelBadge.Height - 1);
            using var pen = new System.Drawing.Pen(System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(60, 59, 130, 246), 1f);
            using var path = CreateRoundedPath(rect, 13);
            e.Graphics.DrawPath(pen, path);
        }

        // Váº½ border bo gÃ³c cho input wrapper (dÃ¹ng chung cho cáº£ 2 input)
        // Border xanh Ä‘áº­m khi control bÃªn trong Ä‘ang focused, xÃ¡m nháº¡t khi khÃ´ng focus
        private void panelInput_Paint(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.PaintEventArgs e)
        {
            var panel   = (System.Windows.Forms.Panel)sender;
            bool focused = panel.ContainsFocus; // true khi TextBox bÃªn trong Ä‘ang focus
            var color = focused
                ? System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(37, 99, 235)   // Xanh khi focus
                : System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(226, 232, 240); // XÃ¡m khi bÃ¬nh thÆ°á»ng
            float width = focused ? 2f : 1.5f;

            e.Graphics.SmoothingMode = System.Drawing.Drawing2D.SmoothingMode.AntiAlias;
            var rect = new System.Drawing.Rectangle(0, 0, panel.Width - 1, panel.Height - 1);
            using var pen  = new System.Drawing.Pen(color, width);
            using var path = CreateRoundedPath(rect, 10);
            e.Graphics.DrawPath(pen, path);
        }

        // Váº½ loading bar gradient (xanh â†’ teal)
        private void panelProgress_Paint(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.PaintEventArgs e)
        {
            if (panelProgress.Width <= 0) return;
            using var brush = new System.Drawing.Drawing2D.LinearGradientBrush(
                new System.Drawing.Rectangle(0, 0, panelProgress.Width, panelProgress.Height),
                System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(37, 99, 235),
                System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(6, 182, 212),
                0f);
            e.Graphics.FillRectangle(brush, 0, 0, panelProgress.Width, panelProgress.Height);
        }

        // Váº½ nÃºt Login: gradient xanh + bo gÃ³c 10px + text cÄƒn giá»¯a
        private void btnLogin_Paint(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.PaintEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Graphics.SmoothingMode = System.Drawing.Drawing2D.SmoothingMode.AntiAlias;
            using var brush = new System.Drawing.Drawing2D.LinearGradientBrush(
                btnLogin.ClientRectangle,
                System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(37, 99, 235),
                System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(29, 78, 216),
                90f);
            using var path = CreateRoundedPath(btnLogin.ClientRectangle, 10);
            e.Graphics.FillPath(brush, path);

            using var sf = new System.Drawing.StringFormat
            {
                Alignment     = System.Drawing.StringAlignment.Center,
                LineAlignment = System.Drawing.StringAlignment.Center
            };
            e.Graphics.DrawString(
                btnLogin.Text, btnLogin.Font,
                System.Drawing.Brushes.White,
                btnLogin.ClientRectangle, sf);
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // HELPER â€“ táº¡o GraphicsPath hÃ¬nh chá»¯ nháº­t bo gÃ³c
        // DÃ¹ng bá»Ÿi táº¥t cáº£ Paint events bÃªn trÃªn
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private static System.Drawing.Drawing2D.GraphicsPath CreateRoundedPath(
            System.Drawing.Rectangle bounds, int radius)
        {
            int d    = radius * 2;
            var path = new System.Drawing.Drawing2D.GraphicsPath();
            path.AddArc(bounds.X,                        bounds.Y,                        d, d, 180, 90);
            path.AddArc(bounds.X + bounds.Width - d,     bounds.Y,                        d, d, 270, 90);
            path.AddArc(bounds.X + bounds.Width - d,     bounds.Y + bounds.Height - d,    d, d,   0, 90);
            path.AddArc(bounds.X,                        bounds.Y + bounds.Height - d,    d, d,  90, 90);
            path.CloseFigure();
            return path;
        }

        // â”€â”€ Control declarations â”€â”€
        private System.Windows.Forms.Panel    panelLeft;
        private System.Windows.Forms.Panel    panelRing1;
        private System.Windows.Forms.Panel    panelRing2;
        private System.Windows.Forms.Panel    panelLogoBox;

        private System.Windows.Forms.Label    lblFeat2;

using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;
using TaskFlowManagement.WinForms.Common;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.WinForms.Forms
{
    public partial class frmMain : Form
    {
        private readonly IServiceProvider _serviceProvider;
        private System.Windows.Forms.Timer? _clockTimer;

        public frmMain(IServiceProvider serviceProvider)
        {
            _serviceProvider = serviceProvider;
            InitializeComponent();
            ApplyRolePermissions();
            StartClock();
            UpdateUserInfo();
        }

        protected override void OnLoad(EventArgs e)
        {
            base.OnLoad(e);
            OpenHome();
        }

        private void OpenHome()
        {
            foreach (Form child in this.MdiChildren) child.Close();
            var home = _serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmHome>();
            home.MdiParent   = this;
            home.WindowState = FormWindowState.Maximized;
            home.Show();
        }

        private void UpdateUserInfo()
        {
            lblStatusUser.Text = $"  ðŸ‘¤ {AppSession.FullName}";
            lblStatusRole.Text = $"  [{string.Join(", ", AppSession.Roles)}]";
            this.Text          = $"TaskFlow  â€”  {AppSession.FullName}";
        }

        // PhÃ¢n quyá»n menu theo Role
        private void ApplyRolePermissions()
        {
            // Reset â€” máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh hiá»‡n táº¥t cáº£
            menuUsers.Visible        = true;
            menuCustomers.Visible    = true;
            menuProjects.Visible     = true;
            menuReports.Visible      = true;
            menuTaskList.Visible     = true;
            menuKanban.Visible       = true;
            menuUserAccounts.Visible = true;

            // FIX GD4: menuMyTasks hiá»‡n cho Má»ŒI role (cáº£ Developer láº«n Manager)
            // Developer cáº§n xem task Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao cho mÃ¬nh â†’ khÃ´ng áº©n menu nÃ y
            menuMyTasks.Visible = true;

            if (!AppSession.IsManager)
            {
                menuUsers.Visible     = false;
                menuCustomers.Visible = false;
                menuReports.Visible   = false;
                // FIX GD4: Developer váº«n tháº¥y menu "Danh sÃ¡ch cÃ´ng viá»‡c" (xem read-only)
                // Trong frmTaskList, ApplyRolePermissions() Ä‘Ã£ áº©n nÃºt ThÃªm/Sá»­a/XÃ³a rá»“i
                // menuTaskList.Visible = false; â† ÄÃƒ Bá»Ž dÃ²ng nÃ y
                menuKanban.Visible    = false;
                menuProjectNew.Visible = false; // Developer khÃ´ng táº¡o dá»± Ã¡n má»›i
            }
            if (!AppSession.IsAdmin)
                menuUserAccounts.Visible = false;
        }

        // Äá»“ng há»“ realtime
        private void StartClock()
        {
            StopClock();
            _clockTimer = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer { Interval = 1000 };
            _clockTimer.Tick += (s, e) =>
                lblStatusTime.Text = DateTime.Now.ToString("HH:mm:ss   dd/MM/yyyy  ");
            _clockTimer.Start();
        }

        private void StopClock()
        {
            if (_clockTimer != null)
            { _clockTimer.Stop(); _clockTimer.Dispose(); _clockTimer = null; }
        }

        // Má»Ÿ MDI child, kiá»ƒm tra trÃ¡nh má»Ÿ trÃ¹ng form cÃ¹ng type
        private void OpenMdiChild(Form child)
        {
            foreach (Form existing in this.MdiChildren)
            {
                if (existing.GetType() == child.GetType())
                { existing.Activate(); child.Dispose(); return; }
            }
            child.MdiParent   = this;
            child.WindowState = FormWindowState.Maximized;
            child.Show();
        }

        // â”€â”€ Menu: Há»‡ thá»‘ng â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private void menuHome_Click(object sender, EventArgs e) => OpenHome();

        private void menuChangePassword_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            var frm = _serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmChangePassword>();
            frm.ShowDialog(this);
        }

        private void menuLogout_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (MessageBox.Show("Báº¡n cÃ³ cháº¯c muá»‘n Ä‘Äƒng xuáº¥t?", "XÃ¡c nháº­n Ä‘Äƒng xuáº¥t",
                    MessageBoxButtons.YesNo, MessageBoxIcon.Question) != DialogResult.Yes)
                return;

            StopClock();
            AppSession.Logout();
            this.Hide();

            var loginForm = _serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmLogin>();
            if (loginForm.ShowDialog() == DialogResult.OK)
            {
                UpdateUserInfo();
                ApplyRolePermissions();
                StartClock();
                this.Show();
                OpenHome();
            }
            else Application.Exit();
        }

        private void menuExit_Click(object sender, EventArgs e) => Application.Exit();

        // â”€â”€ Menu: NgÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private void menuUserAccounts_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => OpenMdiChild(_serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmUsers>());

        private void menuEmployees_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => OpenMdiChild(_serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmUsers>());

        // â”€â”€ Menu: KhÃ¡ch hÃ ng â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private void menuCustomerList_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => OpenMdiChild(_serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmCustomers>());

        // â”€â”€ Menu: Dá»± Ã¡n (GD3) â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private void menuProjectList_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => OpenMdiChild(_serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmProjects>());

        private void menuProjectNew_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => OpenMdiChild(_serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmProjects>());

        // â”€â”€ Menu: CÃ´ng viá»‡c (GD4) â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// Má»Ÿ form Danh sÃ¡ch cÃ´ng viá»‡c â€” GD4.
        /// Manager: tháº¥y táº¥t cáº£ task, cÃ³ nÃºt ThÃªm/Sá»­a/XÃ³a.
        /// Developer: chá»‰ tháº¥y task Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao, khÃ´ng cÃ³ nÃºt CRUD.
        /// </summary>
        private void menuTaskList_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => OpenMdiChild(_serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmTaskList>());

        private void menuKanban_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => ShowComingSoon("Kanban Board", "Giai Ä‘oáº¡n 5");

        /// <summary>
        /// Má»Ÿ form CÃ´ng viá»‡c cá»§a tÃ´i â€” GD4.
        /// Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ task Ä‘Æ°á»£c giao / cáº§n review / cáº§n test cá»§a user Ä‘ang Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p.
        /// </summary>
        private void menuMyTasks_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => OpenMdiChild(_serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<frmMyTasks>());

        // â”€â”€ Menu: BÃ¡o cÃ¡o â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private void menuDashboard_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => ShowComingSoon("Dashboard tá»•ng quan", "Giai Ä‘oáº¡n 6");

        private void menuReportProgress_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => ShowComingSoon("BÃ¡o cÃ¡o tiáº¿n Ä‘á»™", "Giai Ä‘oáº¡n 6");

        private void menuReportBudget_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => ShowComingSoon("BÃ¡o cÃ¡o ngÃ¢n sÃ¡ch", "Giai Ä‘oáº¡n 6");

        private static void ShowComingSoon(string featureName, string phase)
            => MessageBox.Show(
                $"TÃ­nh nÄƒng \"{featureName}\" Ä‘ang Ä‘Æ°á»£c phÃ¡t triá»ƒn.\n\nDá»± kiáº¿n hoÃ n thÃ nh: {phase}.",
                "Äang phÃ¡t triá»ƒn", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Information);

        protected override void OnFormClosing(FormClosingEventArgs e)
        { StopClock(); base.OnFormClosing(e); }
    }

        // DEPENDENCIES
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private readonly ITaskService _taskService = null!;
        private readonly IProjectService _projectService = null!;  // FIX: thÃªm field Ä‘á»ƒ dÃ¹ng trong double-click
        private readonly IUserService _userService = null!;   // FIX: thÃªm field Ä‘á»ƒ dÃ¹ng trong double-click

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // CONSTRUCTORS
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// Constructor máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh â€” Báº®T BUá»˜C Ä‘á»ƒ tab [Design] khÃ´ng lá»—i.
        /// </summary>
        public frmMyTasks()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Constructor DI â€” ServiceProvider gá»i cÃ¡i nÃ y khi cháº¡y tháº­t.
        /// FIX: ThÃªm IProjectService vÃ  IUserService Ä‘á»ƒ má»Ÿ frmTaskEdit khi double-click.
        /// KhÃ´ng cáº§n dÃ¹ng form.Tag ná»¯a â€” inject tháº³ng vÃ o constructor sáº¡ch hÆ¡n.
        /// </summary>
        public frmMyTasks(ITaskService taskService, IProjectService projectService, IUserService userService)
            : this()
        {
            _taskService = taskService;
            _projectService = projectService;
            _userService = userService;
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // FORM LOAD
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        protected override async void OnLoad(EventArgs e)
        {
            base.OnLoad(e);

            this.Text = $"ðŸ“‹ CÃ´ng viá»‡c cá»§a tÃ´i â€” {AppSession.FullName}";
            lblUser.Text = $"Äang hiá»ƒn thá»‹ cÃ´ng viá»‡c cá»§a: {AppSession.FullName} ({AppSession.Username})";

            ApplyRolePermissions();
            await LoadAllTabsAsync();
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // PHÃ‚N QUYá»€N THEO ROLE
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private void ApplyRolePermissions()
        {
            // Developer khÃ´ng thá»±c hiá»‡n Review/Test â†’ áº©n 2 tab Ä‘Ã³
            bool canReviewOrTest = AppSession.IsManager;
            tabReview.Parent = canReviewOrTest ? tabControl : null;
            tabTesting.Parent = canReviewOrTest ? tabControl : null;
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // LOAD Dá»® LIá»†U Cáº¢ 3 TAB
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private async Task LoadAllTabsAsync()
        {
            lblStatus.Text = "Äang táº£i...";

            try
            {
                // Load song song 4 nguá»“n Ä‘á»ƒ tiáº¿t kiá»‡m thá»i gian chá»
                var tMine = _taskService.GetMyTasksAsync(AppSession.UserId);
                var tReview1 = _taskService.GetTasksForReviewer1Async(AppSession.UserId);
                var tReview2 = _taskService.GetTasksForReviewer2Async(AppSession.UserId);
                var tTest = _taskService.GetTasksForTesterAsync(AppSession.UserId);

                await Task.WhenAll(tMine, tReview1, tReview2, tTest);

                // Gá»™p Review1 + Review2 vÃ o 1 tab
                var reviewTasks = tReview1.Result.Concat(tReview2.Result).ToList();

                BindGrid(dgvMyTasks, tMine.Result);
                BindGrid(dgvReview, reviewTasks);
                BindGrid(dgvTesting, tTest.Result);

                // Cáº­p nháº­t sá»‘ lÆ°á»£ng task lÃªn tiÃªu Ä‘á» tab
                tabMyTasks.Text = $"ðŸ“‹ ÄÆ°á»£c giao ({tMine.Result.Count})";
                tabReview.Text = $"ðŸ” Review ({reviewTasks.Count})";
                tabTesting.Text = $"ðŸ§ª Testing ({tTest.Result.Count})";

                int total = tMine.Result.Count + reviewTasks.Count + tTest.Result.Count;
                lblStatus.Text = $"Tá»•ng cá»™ng {total} cÃ´ng viá»‡c liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n báº¡n.";
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                lblStatus.Text = "Lá»—i táº£i dá»¯ liá»‡u.";
                MessageBox.Show("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº£i dá»¯ liá»‡u:\n" + ex.Message,
                    "Lá»—i", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
            }
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // BIND Dá»® LIá»†U VÃ€O DATAGRIDVIEW
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private static void BindGrid(DataGridView dgv, List<TaskItem> items)
        {
            dgv.Rows.Clear();

            foreach (var t in items)
            {
                var due = t.DueDate.HasValue
                    ? t.DueDate.Value.ToLocalTime().ToString("dd/MM/yyyy")
                    : "â€”";

                // Thá»© tá»± cá»™t: colId | colTitle | colProject | colPriority | colStatus | colProgress | colDueDate
                int idx = dgv.Rows.Add(
                    t.Id,
                    t.Title,
                    t.Project?.Name ?? "â€”",
                    t.Priority?.Name ?? "â€”",
                    t.Status?.Name ?? "â€”",
                    $"{t.ProgressPercent}%",
                    due);

                ApplyRowColor(dgv.Rows[idx], t);
            }
        }

        private static void ApplyRowColor(DataGridViewRow row, TaskItem task)
        {
            if (task.DueDate.HasValue && task.DueDate.Value < DateTime.UtcNow && !task.IsCompleted)
            {
                row.DefaultCellStyle.ForeColor = Color.FromArgb(185, 28, 28);
                return;
            }

            row.DefaultCellStyle.ForeColor = task.Status?.Name switch
            {
                "CLOSED" => Color.FromArgb(5, 150, 105),
                "RESOLVED" => Color.FromArgb(22, 163, 74),
                "FAILED" => Color.FromArgb(220, 38, 38),
                "IN-PROGRESS" => Color.FromArgb(37, 99, 235),
                "REVIEW-1" or "REVIEW-2" => Color.FromArgb(180, 83, 9),
                "IN-TEST" => Color.FromArgb(109, 40, 217),
                _ => Color.FromArgb(30, 41, 59),
            };
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // NÃšT LÃ€M Má»šI
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private async void btnRefresh_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            await LoadAllTabsAsync();
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // Má»ž FORM Sá»¬A KHI DOUBLE-CLICK
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>
        /// Double-click vÃ o báº¥t ká»³ DataGridView nÃ o â†’ má»Ÿ frmTaskEdit Ä‘á»ƒ xem/sá»­a chi tiáº¿t.
        /// FIX: DÃ¹ng _projectService vÃ  _userService Ä‘Ã£ inject vÃ o constructor,
        ///      khÃ´ng cáº§n truyá»n qua form.Tag ná»¯a â†’ sáº¡ch hÆ¡n, khÃ´ng cÃ²n lá»—i thiáº¿u tham sá»‘.
        /// </summary>
        private void dgv_CellDoubleClick(object sender, DataGridViewCellEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.RowIndex < 0) return;
            if (sender is not DataGridView dgv) return;

            var cell = dgv.Rows[e.RowIndex].Cells["colId"].Value;
            if (cell == null) return;

            int taskId = (int)cell;

            // FIX: truyá»n Ä‘á»§ 4 tham sá»‘ theo constructor má»›i cá»§a frmTaskEdit
            using var dlg = new frmTaskEdit(_taskService, _projectService, _userService, taskId);
            if (dlg.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
                _ = LoadAllTabsAsync(); // Reload sau khi sá»­a xong
        }
    }
}

        /// <summary>
        /// Cáº¥u hÃ¬nh DataGridView theo chuáº©n chung cá»§a GD4.
        /// Gá»i cho cáº£ 3 grid Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh láº·p code.
        /// Táº¥t cáº£ cá»™t Ä‘á»u dÃ¹ng tÃªn prefix "col" Ä‘á»ƒ BindGrid() tham chiáº¿u.
        /// </summary>
        private static void ConfigureTaskGrid(DataGridView dgv)
        {
            dgv.AutoGenerateColumns   = false;
            dgv.SelectionMode         = DataGridViewSelectionMode.FullRowSelect;
            dgv.MultiSelect           = false;
            dgv.ReadOnly              = true;
            dgv.AllowUserToAddRows    = false;
            dgv.AllowUserToDeleteRows = false;
            dgv.RowHeadersVisible     = false;
            dgv.Font                  = new Font("Segoe UI", 9.5F);
            dgv.ColumnHeadersHeight   = 36;
            dgv.RowTemplate.Height    = 30;

            // â”€â”€ Äá»‹nh nghÄ©a cá»™t â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            var colId = new DataGridViewTextBoxColumn
            {
                Name        = "colId",
                HeaderText  = "ID",
                Width       = 50,
                Visible     = false  // áº©n, chá»‰ dÃ¹ng Ä‘á»ƒ tra Id khi xá»­ lÃ½ sá»± kiá»‡n
            };
            var colTitle = new DataGridViewTextBoxColumn
            {
                Name         = "colTitle",
                HeaderText   = "TiÃªu Ä‘á» cÃ´ng viá»‡c",
                AutoSizeMode = DataGridViewAutoSizeColumnMode.Fill,
                MinimumWidth = 200
            };
            var colProject = new DataGridViewTextBoxColumn
            {
                Name       = "colProject",
                HeaderText = "Dá»± Ã¡n",
                Width      = 140
            };
            var colPriority = new DataGridViewTextBoxColumn
            {
                Name       = "colPriority",
                HeaderText = "Æ¯u tiÃªn",
                Width      = 85
            };
            var colStatus = new DataGridViewTextBoxColumn
            {
                Name       = "colStatus",
                HeaderText = "Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i",
                Width      = 110
            };
            var colProgress = new DataGridViewTextBoxColumn
            {
                Name       = "colProgress",
                HeaderText = "%",
                Width      = 55,
                DefaultCellStyle = { Alignment = DataGridViewContentAlignment.MiddleCenter }
            };
            var colDueDate = new DataGridViewTextBoxColumn
            {
                Name       = "colDueDate",
                HeaderText = "Háº¡n chÃ³t",
                Width      = 95
            };

            dgv.Columns.AddRange(new DataGridViewColumn[]
            {
                colId, colTitle, colProject, colPriority, colStatus, colProgress, colDueDate
            });
        }

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;
using TaskFlowManagement.WinForms.Common;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.WinForms.Forms
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Form thÃªm/sá»­a dá»± Ã¡n.
    /// ThÃªm má»›i: nháº­p tÃªn, khÃ¡ch hÃ ng, PM, ngÃ y, deadline, ngÃ¢n sÃ¡ch, priority.
    /// Sá»­a: load data hiá»‡n táº¡i vÃ o form, cho phÃ©p chá»‰nh sá»­a.
    /// </summary>
    public partial class frmProjectEdit : Form
    {
        private readonly IProjectService _projectService;
        private readonly IUserService _userService;
        private readonly ICustomerRepository _customerRepo;
        private readonly Project? _editProject;
        private readonly bool _isEdit;

        private List<Customer> _customers = new();
        private List<User> _managers = new();

        public frmProjectEdit(IProjectService projectService, IUserService userService,
            ICustomerRepository customerRepo, Project? editProject)
        {
            _projectService = projectService;
            _userService    = userService;
            _customerRepo   = customerRepo;
            _editProject    = editProject;
            _isEdit         = editProject != null;
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        protected override async void OnLoad(EventArgs e)
        {
            base.OnLoad(e);
            await LoadDropdownsAsync();
            if (_isEdit) LoadEditData();
        }

        /// <summary>Load danh sÃ¡ch khÃ¡ch hÃ ng, managers, priority vÃ o cÃ¡c dropdown.</summary>
        private async Task LoadDropdownsAsync()
        {
            // KhÃ¡ch hÃ ng
            _customers = await _customerRepo.GetAllAsync();
            cboCustomer.Items.Clear();
            cboCustomer.Items.Add("â€” KhÃ´ng chá»n â€”");
            foreach (var c in _customers)
                cboCustomer.Items.Add(c.CompanyName);
            cboCustomer.SelectedIndex = 0;

            // Managers (Admin + Manager) lÃ m PM
            var allUsers = await _userService.GetAllUsersAsync();
            _managers = allUsers.Where(u => u.IsActive &&
                u.UserRoles.Any(r => r.Role?.Name == "Manager" || r.Role?.Name == "Admin")).ToList();
            cboOwner.Items.Clear();
            foreach (var m in _managers)
                cboOwner.Items.Add(m.FullName);
            if (cboOwner.Items.Count > 0) cboOwner.SelectedIndex = 0;

            // Priority
            cboPriority.Items.AddRange(new object[] { "Low", "Medium", "High", "Critical" });
            cboPriority.SelectedIndex = 1;
        }

        /// <summary>Load dá»¯ liá»‡u dá»± Ã¡n hiá»‡n táº¡i vÃ o form khi cháº¿ Ä‘á»™ sá»­a.</summary>
        private void LoadEditData()
        {
            this.Text         = "Sá»­a thÃ´ng tin dá»± Ã¡n";
            lblTitleForm.Text = "âœï¸  Sá»­a thÃ´ng tin dá»± Ã¡n";

            txtName.Text        = _editProject!.Name;
            txtDescription.Text = _editProject.Description ?? "";
            dtpStartDate.Value  = _editProject.StartDate.ToDateTime(TimeOnly.MinValue);
            if (_editProject.PlannedEndDate.HasValue)
            {
                chkDeadline.Checked = true;
                dtpDeadline.Value   = _editProject.PlannedEndDate.Value.ToDateTime(TimeOnly.MinValue);
            }
            txtBudget.Text = _editProject.Budget > 0 ? _editProject.Budget.ToString("0") : "";

            // Chá»n khÃ¡ch hÃ ng trong dropdown
            if (_editProject.CustomerId.HasValue)
            {
                var idx = _customers.FindIndex(c => c.Id == _editProject.CustomerId);
                cboCustomer.SelectedIndex = idx >= 0 ? idx + 1 : 0;
            }

            // Chá»n PM
            var ownerIdx = _managers.FindIndex(m => m.Id == _editProject.OwnerId);
            if (ownerIdx >= 0) cboOwner.SelectedIndex = ownerIdx;

            // Chá»n priority
            cboPriority.SelectedIndex = Math.Max(0, _editProject.Priority - 1);
        }

        /// <summary>LÆ°u dá»± Ã¡n (táº¡o má»›i hoáº·c cáº­p nháº­t) sau khi validate.</summary>
        private async void btnSave_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            lblError.Text = "";

            // â”€â”€ Validate â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtName.Text))
            { lblError.Text = "âš   TÃªn dá»± Ã¡n khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»ƒ trá»‘ng."; txtName.Focus(); return; }

            if (cboOwner.SelectedIndex < 0)
            { lblError.Text = "âš   Vui lÃ²ng chá»n ngÆ°á»i quáº£n lÃ½."; return; }

            // Validate deadline pháº£i sau ngÃ y báº¯t Ä‘áº§u
            if (chkDeadline.Checked && dtpDeadline.Value.Date <= dtpStartDate.Value.Date)
            {
                lblError.Text = "âš   Deadline pháº£i sau ngÃ y báº¯t Ä‘áº§u.";
                dtpDeadline.Focus();
                return;
            }

            SetLoading(true);
            try
            {
                int? customerId = cboCustomer.SelectedIndex > 0
                    ? _customers[cboCustomer.SelectedIndex - 1].Id : null;
                int ownerId = _managers[cboOwner.SelectedIndex].Id;

                // Parse ngÃ¢n sÃ¡ch (bá» dáº¥u phÃ¢n cÃ¡ch)
                decimal budget = 0;
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtBudget.Text))
                    decimal.TryParse(txtBudget.Text.Replace(",", "").Replace(".", ""), out budget);

                DateOnly? deadline = chkDeadline.Checked
                    ? DateOnly.FromDateTime(dtpDeadline.Value) : null;

                if (_isEdit)
                {
                    _editProject!.Name          = txtName.Text.Trim();
                    _editProject.Description    = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtDescription.Text) ? null : txtDescription.Text.Trim();
                    _editProject.CustomerId     = customerId;
                    _editProject.OwnerId        = ownerId;
                    _editProject.StartDate      = DateOnly.FromDateTime(dtpStartDate.Value);
                    _editProject.PlannedEndDate = deadline;
                    _editProject.Budget         = budget;
                    _editProject.Priority       = (byte)(cboPriority.SelectedIndex + 1);

                    var (ok, msg) = await _projectService.UpdateProjectAsync(_editProject);
                    SetLoading(false);
                    if (ok) { this.DialogResult = DialogResult.OK; this.Close(); }
                    else lblError.Text = "âš   " + msg;
                }
                else
                {
                    var project = new Project
                    {
                        Name           = txtName.Text.Trim(),
                        Description    = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtDescription.Text) ? null : txtDescription.Text.Trim(),
                        CustomerId     = customerId,
                        OwnerId        = ownerId,
                        StartDate      = DateOnly.FromDateTime(dtpStartDate.Value),
                        PlannedEndDate = deadline,
                        Budget         = budget,
                        Priority       = (byte)(cboPriority.SelectedIndex + 1),
                        Status         = "NotStarted"
                    };
                    var (ok, msg) = await _projectService.CreateProjectAsync(project);
                    SetLoading(false);
                    if (ok) { this.DialogResult = DialogResult.OK; this.Close(); }
                    else lblError.Text = "âš   " + msg;
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                SetLoading(false);
                lblError.Text = "âš   Lá»—i: " + (ex.InnerException?.Message ?? ex.Message);
            }
        }

        private void btnCancel_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        { this.DialogResult = DialogResult.Cancel; this.Close(); }

        /// <summary>Báº­t/táº¯t DateTimePicker deadline theo checkbox.</summary>
        private void chkDeadline_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        { dtpDeadline.Enabled = chkDeadline.Checked; }

        private void SetLoading(bool loading)
        { btnSave.Enabled = !loading; btnSave.Text = loading ? "Äang lÆ°u..." : "ðŸ’¾  LÆ°u"; }
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;
using TaskFlowManagement.WinForms.Common;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.WinForms.Forms
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Quáº£n lÃ½ thÃ nh viÃªn dá»± Ã¡n â€“ thÃªm developer, gÃ¡n vai trÃ², xÃ³a (soft delete).
    /// </summary>
    public partial class frmProjectMembers : Form
    {
        private readonly IProjectService _projectService;
        private readonly IUserService _userService;
        private readonly Project _project;
        private List<ProjectMember> _members = new();
        private List<User> _availableUsers = new();

        public frmProjectMembers(IProjectService projectService, IUserService userService, Project project)
        {
            _projectService = projectService;
            _userService    = userService;
            _project        = project;
            InitializeComponent();
            lblTitle.Text = $"ðŸ‘¥  ThÃ nh viÃªn â€” {_project.Name}";

            // Developer chá»‰ xem, khÃ´ng thÃªm/xÃ³a
            bool canEdit = AppSession.IsManager;
            panelAdd.Visible  = canEdit;
            btnRemove.Visible = canEdit;
        }

        protected override async void OnLoad(EventArgs e)
        {
            base.OnLoad(e);
            await LoadMembersAsync();
            await LoadAvailableUsersAsync();

            // Load danh sÃ¡ch vai trÃ² trong dá»± Ã¡n
            cboProjectRole.Items.AddRange(new object[] { "Developer", "Tester", "BA", "Tech Lead" });
            cboProjectRole.SelectedIndex = 0;
        }

        // Load thÃ nh viÃªn hiá»‡n táº¡i
        private async Task LoadMembersAsync()
        {
            _members = await _projectService.GetMembersAsync(_project.Id);
            dgvMembers.Rows.Clear();
            foreach (var m in _members)
            {
                dgvMembers.Rows.Add(
                    m.UserId,
                    m.User?.FullName ?? "â€”",
                    m.User?.Email ?? "â€”",
                    m.ProjectRole ?? "â€”",
                    m.JoinedAt.ToLocalTime().ToString("dd/MM/yyyy"));
            }
            lblCount.Text = $"{_members.Count} thÃ nh viÃªn";
        }

        // Load user chÆ°a trong dá»± Ã¡n Ä‘á»ƒ thÃªm
        private async Task LoadAvailableUsersAsync()
        {
            var allActive = await _userService.GetAllActiveUsersAsync();
            var memberIds = _members.Select(m => m.UserId).ToHashSet();
            _availableUsers = allActive.Where(u => !memberIds.Contains(u.Id)).ToList();

            cboUser.Items.Clear();
            foreach (var u in _availableUsers)
                cboUser.Items.Add($"{u.FullName}  ({u.Username})");
            if (cboUser.Items.Count > 0) cboUser.SelectedIndex = 0;
        }

        // ThÃªm thÃ nh viÃªn
        private async void btnAddMember_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (cboUser.SelectedIndex < 0)
            { MessageBox.Show("Vui lÃ²ng chá»n ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng.", "ThÃ´ng bÃ¡o", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning); return; }

            var user = _availableUsers[cboUser.SelectedIndex];
            var role = cboProjectRole.SelectedItem?.ToString() ?? "Developer";

            var (ok, msg) = await _projectService.AddMemberAsync(_project.Id, user.Id, role);
            if (ok)
            {
                await LoadMembersAsync();
                await LoadAvailableUsersAsync();
            }
            else
            {
                MessageBox.Show(msg, "Lá»—i", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
            }
        }

        // XÃ³a thÃ nh viÃªn (soft delete)
        private async void btnRemove_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (dgvMembers.SelectedRows.Count == 0) return;
            int userId = (int)dgvMembers.SelectedRows[0].Cells["colMemberId"].Value;
            var member = _members.FirstOrDefault(m => m.UserId == userId);
            if (member == null) return;

            if (MessageBox.Show(
                $"XÃ³a \"{member.User?.FullName}\" khá»i dá»± Ã¡n?\n\nLá»‹ch sá»­ tham gia váº«n Ä‘Æ°á»£c lÆ°u láº¡i.",
                "XÃ¡c nháº­n", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo, MessageBoxIcon.Question) != DialogResult.Yes) return;

            var (ok, msg) = await _projectService.RemoveMemberAsync(_project.Id, userId);
            if (ok)
            {
                await LoadMembersAsync();
                await LoadAvailableUsersAsync();
            }
        }

        private void btnClose_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        { this.Close(); }
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;
using TaskFlowManagement.WinForms.Common;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.WinForms.Forms
{
    /// <summary>
    /// MÃ n hÃ¬nh danh sÃ¡ch dá»± Ã¡n.
    /// Manager/Admin: táº¡o, sá»­a, xÃ³a, Ä‘á»•i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i, quáº£n lÃ½ thÃ nh viÃªn.
    /// Developer: chá»‰ xem dá»± Ã¡n mÃ¬nh tham gia (read-only).
    /// </summary>
    public partial class frmProjects : Form
    {
        private readonly IProjectService _projectService;
        private readonly IUserService _userService;
        private readonly ICustomerRepository _customerRepo;
        private List<Project> _allProjects = new();
        private Project? _selectedProject;

        public frmProjects(IProjectService projectService, IUserService userService,
            ICustomerRepository customerRepo)
        {
            _projectService = projectService;
            _userService    = userService;
            _customerRepo   = customerRepo;
            InitializeComponent();
            SetupPermissions();
        }

        /// <summary>áº¨n nÃºt CRUD náº¿u Developer (chá»‰ xem, khÃ´ng chá»‰nh sá»­a).</summary>
        private void SetupPermissions()
        {
            bool canEdit = AppSession.IsManager;
            btnAdd.Visible    = canEdit;
            btnEdit.Visible   = canEdit;
            btnDelete.Visible = canEdit;
            btnStatus.Visible = canEdit;
        }

        protected override async void OnLoad(EventArgs e)
        {
            base.OnLoad(e);
            await LoadProjectsAsync();
        }

        /// <summary>Load danh sÃ¡ch dá»± Ã¡n tá»« DB theo quyá»n user hiá»‡n táº¡i.</summary>
        private async Task LoadProjectsAsync()
        {
            SetStatus("Äang táº£i...");
            _allProjects = await _projectService.GetProjectsForUserAsync(
                AppSession.UserId, AppSession.IsManager);

            // Load chi tiáº¿t members cho má»—i project Ä‘á»ƒ Ä‘áº¿m thÃ nh viÃªn
            for (int i = 0; i < _allProjects.Count; i++)
            {
                var detail = await _projectService.GetProjectDetailsAsync(_allProjects[i].Id);
                if (detail != null) _allProjects[i] = detail;
            }

            ApplyFilter();
            SetStatus($"Tá»•ng: {_allProjects.Count} dá»± Ã¡n");
        }

        /// <summary>Lá»c danh sÃ¡ch theo tá»« khÃ³a tÃ¬m kiáº¿m vÃ  tráº¡ng thÃ¡i.</summary>
        private void ApplyFilter()
        {
            var keyword = txtSearch.Text.Trim().ToLower();
            var statusFilter = cboFilterStatus.SelectedIndex > 0
                ? cboFilterStatus.SelectedItem!.ToString()! : "";

            var filtered = _allProjects.Where(p =>
            {
                bool matchKeyword = string.IsNullOrEmpty(keyword)
                    || p.Name.ToLower().Contains(keyword)
                    || (p.Customer?.CompanyName?.ToLower().Contains(keyword) ?? false)
                    || (p.Owner?.FullName?.ToLower().Contains(keyword) ?? false);

                bool matchStatus = string.IsNullOrEmpty(statusFilter)
                    || p.Status == statusFilter;

                return matchKeyword && matchStatus;
            }).ToList();

            BindGrid(filtered);
        }

        /// <summary>Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ danh sÃ¡ch dá»± Ã¡n lÃªn DataGridView vá»›i tÃ´ mÃ u theo tráº¡ng thÃ¡i.</summary>
        private void BindGrid(List<Project> projects)
        {
            dgvProjects.Rows.Clear();
            foreach (var p in projects)
            {
                // Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ tráº¡ng thÃ¡i kÃ¨m icon
                var statusText = p.Status switch
                {
                    "NotStarted" => "ðŸ“‹ ChÆ°a báº¯t Ä‘áº§u",
                    "InProgress" => "ðŸ”„ Äang thá»±c hiá»‡n",
                    "OnHold"     => "â¸ Táº¡m dá»«ng",
                    "Completed"  => "âœ… HoÃ n thÃ nh",
                    "Cancelled"  => "âŒ ÄÃ£ há»§y",
                    _            => p.Status
                };

                var deadline = p.PlannedEndDate.HasValue
                    ? p.PlannedEndDate.Value.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy") : "â€”";

                var budget = p.Budget > 0
                    ? p.Budget.ToString("N0") + " â‚«" : "â€”";

                // Äáº¿m thÃ nh viÃªn active
                var memberCount = p.Members?.Count(m => m.LeftAt == null) ?? 0;

                int idx = dgvProjects.Rows.Add(
                    p.Id, p.Name, p.Customer?.CompanyName ?? "â€”",
                    p.Owner?.FullName ?? "â€”", statusText,
                    $"{memberCount} ngÆ°á»i",
                    deadline, budget,
                    p.StartDate.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy"));

                // TÃ´ mÃ u theo tráº¡ng thÃ¡i
                var row = dgvProjects.Rows[idx];
                if (p.Status == "Completed")
                    row.DefaultCellStyle.ForeColor = System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(5, 150, 105);
                else if (p.Status == "Cancelled")
                {
                    row.DefaultCellStyle.ForeColor = System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(148, 163, 184);
                    row.DefaultCellStyle.Font = new System.Drawing.Font("Segoe UI", 9.5F, System.Drawing.FontStyle.Italic);
                }
                // Highlight Ä‘á» náº¿u quÃ¡ deadline mÃ  chÆ°a hoÃ n thÃ nh
                else if (p.PlannedEndDate.HasValue
                    && p.PlannedEndDate.Value < DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Now)
                    && p.Status != "Completed")
                    row.DefaultCellStyle.ForeColor = System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(220, 38, 38);
            }
            lblCount.Text = $"{projects.Count} dá»± Ã¡n";
        }

        /// <summary>Cáº­p nháº­t tráº¡ng thÃ¡i nÃºt khi chá»n dÃ²ng khÃ¡c trÃªn grid.</summary>
        private void dgvProjects_SelectionChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (dgvProjects.SelectedRows.Count == 0) { _selectedProject = null; UpdateButtons(); return; }
            int id = (int)dgvProjects.SelectedRows[0].Cells["colId"].Value;
            _selectedProject = _allProjects.FirstOrDefault(p => p.Id == id);
            UpdateButtons();
        }

        private void UpdateButtons()
        {
            bool sel = _selectedProject != null;
            btnEdit.Enabled    = sel;
            btnDelete.Enabled  = sel;
            btnMembers.Enabled = sel;
            btnStatus.Enabled  = sel;
            btnDetail.Enabled  = sel;
        }

        // â”€â”€ ThÃªm dá»± Ã¡n má»›i â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private async void btnAdd_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            using var dlg = new frmProjectEdit(_projectService, _userService, _customerRepo, null);
            if (dlg.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
                await LoadProjectsAsync();
        }

        // â”€â”€ Sá»­a dá»± Ã¡n â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private async void btnEdit_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_selectedProject == null) return;
            var detail = await _projectService.GetProjectDetailsAsync(_selectedProject.Id);
            if (detail == null) return;
            using var dlg = new frmProjectEdit(_projectService, _userService, _customerRepo, detail);
            if (dlg.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
                await LoadProjectsAsync();
        }

        // â”€â”€ XÃ³a dá»± Ã¡n (chá»‰ khi chÆ°a cÃ³ task) â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private async void btnDelete_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_selectedProject == null) return;
            if (MessageBox.Show(
                $"XÃ³a dá»± Ã¡n \"{_selectedProject.Name}\"?\n\nChá»‰ xÃ³a Ä‘Æ°á»£c náº¿u dá»± Ã¡n chÆ°a cÃ³ cÃ´ng viá»‡c nÃ o.",
                "XÃ¡c nháº­n xÃ³a", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo, MessageBoxIcon.Warning) != DialogResult.Yes) return;

            var (ok, msg) = await _projectService.DeleteProjectAsync(_selectedProject.Id);
            MessageBox.Show(msg, ok ? "ThÃ nh cÃ´ng" : "KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ xÃ³a",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK, ok ? MessageBoxIcon.Information : MessageBoxIcon.Error);
            if (ok) await LoadProjectsAsync();
        }

        // â”€â”€ Äá»•i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i dá»± Ã¡n â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private async void btnStatus_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_selectedProject == null) return;
            var menu = new ContextMenuStrip();
            var statuses = new[] { "NotStarted", "InProgress", "OnHold", "Completed", "Cancelled" };
            foreach (var s in statuses)
            {
                var status = s;
                var item = menu.Items.Add(status);
                item.Click += async (_, _) =>
                {
                    var (ok, msg) = await _projectService.ChangeStatusAsync(_selectedProject.Id, status);
                    if (ok) await LoadProjectsAsync();
                    else MessageBox.Show(msg, "Lá»—i", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
                };
            }
            menu.Show(btnStatus, new System.Drawing.Point(0, btnStatus.Height));
        }

        // â”€â”€ Quáº£n lÃ½ thÃ nh viÃªn â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private async void btnMembers_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_selectedProject == null) return;
            using var dlg = new frmProjectMembers(_projectService, _userService, _selectedProject);
            dlg.ShowDialog(this);
            await LoadProjectsAsync();
        }

        // â”€â”€ Chi tiáº¿t dá»± Ã¡n (UC-15) â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private async void btnDetail_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_selectedProject == null) return;
            var detail = await _projectService.GetProjectDetailsAsync(_selectedProject.Id);
            if (detail == null) { MessageBox.Show("KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y dá»± Ã¡n.", "Lá»—i"); return; }

            // Tá»•ng há»£p thÃ´ng tin chi tiáº¿t
            var memberCount = detail.Members?.Count(m => m.LeftAt == null) ?? 0;
            var taskCount   = detail.Tasks?.Count ?? 0;
            var totalExpense = detail.Expenses?.Sum(ex => ex.Amount) ?? 0;
            var progress    = detail.ProgressPercent;

            var memberList = detail.Members?
                .Where(m => m.LeftAt == null)
                .Select(m => $"  ðŸ‘¤ {m.User?.FullName ?? "?"} â€” {m.ProjectRole ?? "Developer"}")
                .ToList() ?? new();

            var info = $"ðŸ“  {detail.Name}\n" +
                $"â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”\n\n" +
                $"KhÃ¡ch hÃ ng:   {detail.Customer?.CompanyName ?? "â€”"}\n" +
                $"Quáº£n lÃ½:        {detail.Owner?.FullName ?? "â€”"}\n" +
                $"Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i:    {detail.Status}\n" +
                $"NgÃ y báº¯t Ä‘áº§u: {detail.StartDate:dd/MM/yyyy}\n" +
                $"Deadline:       {(detail.PlannedEndDate.HasValue ? detail.PlannedEndDate.Value.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy") : "â€”")}\n" +
                $"NgÃ¢n sÃ¡ch:    {detail.Budget:N0} â‚«\n" +
                $"Chi phÃ­ thá»±c:  {totalExpense:N0} â‚«\n" +
                $"Tiáº¿n Ä‘á»™:        {progress}%\n\n" +
                $"â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”\n" +
                $"ðŸ‘¥  ThÃ nh viÃªn ({memberCount})\n" +
                (memberList.Count > 0 ? string.Join("\n", memberList) : "  ChÆ°a cÃ³ thÃ nh viÃªn") +
                $"\n\nðŸ“‹  CÃ´ng viá»‡c: {taskCount} task" +
                (taskCount > 0 ? " (chi tiáº¿t sáº½ cÃ³ á»Ÿ Giai Ä‘oáº¡n 4)" : "");

            MessageBox.Show(info, "Chi tiáº¿t dá»± Ã¡n", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Information);
        }

        // â”€â”€ Filter & Search â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private void txtSearch_TextChanged(object sender, EventArgs e) => ApplyFilter();
        private void cboFilterStatus_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e) => ApplyFilter();
        private async void btnRefresh_Click(object sender, EventArgs e) => await LoadProjectsAsync();

        /// <summary>Double-click má»Ÿ form sá»­a (chá»‰ Manager/Admin).</summary>
        private void dgvProjects_CellDoubleClick(object sender, DataGridViewCellEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.RowIndex >= 0)
            {
                if (AppSession.IsManager) btnEdit_Click(sender, e);
                else btnDetail_Click(sender, e); // Developer double-click â†’ xem chi tiáº¿t
            }
        }

        private void SetStatus(string msg) => lblStatus.Text = msg;
    }
}

        /// <summary>Helper táº¡o toolbar button Ä‘á»“ng bá»™ style.</summary>
        private void SetToolButton(Button btn, string text, System.Drawing.Color bgColor, int x, int y, int w, int h)
        {
            btn.BackColor = bgColor;
            btn.Cursor = Cursors.Hand;
            btn.FlatStyle = FlatStyle.Flat;
            btn.FlatAppearance.BorderSize = 0;
            btn.Font = new System.Drawing.Font("Segoe UI", 9F, System.Drawing.FontStyle.Bold);
            btn.ForeColor = System.Drawing.Color.White;
            btn.Location = new System.Drawing.Point(x, y);
            btn.Size = new System.Drawing.Size(w, h);
            btn.Text = text;
        }

    /// <summary>
    /// Form ThÃªm má»›i / Sá»­a cÃ´ng viá»‡c (TaskItem).
    ///   taskId == null â†’ cháº¿ Ä‘á»™ ThÃªm má»›i
    ///   taskId cÃ³ giÃ¡ trá»‹ â†’ cháº¿ Ä‘á»™ Sá»­a
    ///
    /// DROPDOWN ASSIGNEE:
    ///   Load toÃ n bá»™ user active qua GetAllActiveUsersAsync() â€” khÃ´ng lá»c theo ProjectMember.
    ///   LÃ½ do: seed data cÃ³ thá»ƒ thiáº¿u member trong ProjectMembers â†’ lá»c sáº½ lÃ m dropdown rá»—ng.
    ///   Admin/Manager tá»± chá»‹u trÃ¡ch nhiá»‡m chá»n Ä‘Ãºng ngÆ°á»i.
    ///
    /// PHÃ‚N QUYá»€N COMBOBOX (cháº¿ Ä‘á»™ Sá»­a):
    ///   | Role                      | cboStatus | cboPriority | cboAssignee |
    ///   |---------------------------|-----------|-------------|-------------|
    ///   | Admin / Manager           |   âœ…      |    âœ…       |    âœ…       |
    ///   | Developer (assignee)      |   âœ…      |    âŒ       |    âœ…       |
    ///   | Developer (khÃ´ng assignee)|   âŒ      |    âŒ       |    âŒ       |
    ///
    /// SO SÃNH ROLE: OrdinalIgnoreCase â€” DB seed "Admin"/"Manager"/"Developer"
    /// </summary>
    public partial class frmTaskEdit : Form
    {
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // DEPENDENCIES & STATE
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        private readonly ITaskService    _taskService    = null!;
        private readonly IProjectService _projectService = null!;
        private readonly IUserService    _userService    = null!;

        private readonly int? _taskId;
        private TaskItem?     _editingTask;

        private List<Priority> _priorities = new();
        private List<Status>   _statuses   = new();
        private List<Category> _categories = new();
        private List<Project>  _projects   = new();
        private List<User>     _users      = new();

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // CONSTRUCTORS
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        // Constructor máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh â€” Báº®T BUá»˜C Ä‘á»ƒ tab [Design] khÃ´ng lá»—i
        public frmTaskEdit()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        // Constructor DI â€” dÃ¹ng khi cháº¡y tháº­t
        public frmTaskEdit(
            ITaskService    taskService,
            IProjectService projectService,
            IUserService    userService,
            int?            taskId)
            : this()
        {
            _taskService    = taskService;
            _projectService = projectService;
            _userService    = userService;
            _taskId         = taskId;
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // FORM LOAD
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        protected override async void OnLoad(EventArgs e)
        {
            base.OnLoad(e);
            this.Text = _taskId.HasValue ? $"âœï¸ Sá»­a cÃ´ng viá»‡c (ID: {_taskId.Value})" : "âž• ThÃªm cÃ´ng viá»‡c má»›i";

            await LoadLookupsAsync();

            if (_taskId.HasValue)
                await LoadTaskForEditAsync(_taskId.Value);
            else
                SetDefaultsForNewTask();
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // LOAD LOOKUP DATA
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private async Task LoadLookupsAsync()
        {
            try
            {
                // Load song song 5 nguá»“n
                var tPriorities = _taskService.GetAllPrioritiesAsync();
                var tStatuses   = _taskService.GetAllStatusesAsync();
                var tCategories = _taskService.GetAllCategoriesAsync();
                var tProjects   = _projectService.GetProjectsForUserAsync(
                                      AppSession.UserId, AppSession.IsManager);
                // Láº¥y Táº¤T Cáº¢ user active â€” khÃ´ng lá»c theo ProjectMember
                // Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh dropdown rá»—ng khi seed data thiáº¿u member
                var tUsers = _userService.GetAllActiveUsersAsync();

                await Task.WhenAll(tPriorities, tStatuses, tCategories, tProjects, tUsers);

                _priorities = tPriorities.Result;
                _statuses   = tStatuses.Result;
                _categories = tCategories.Result;
                _projects   = tProjects.Result;
                _users      = tUsers.Result;

                // cboPriority
                cboPriority.Items.Clear();
                cboPriority.Items.Add(new ComboItem(0, "â€” Chá»n má»©c Æ°u tiÃªn â€”"));
                foreach (var p in _priorities.OrderBy(p => p.Level))
                    cboPriority.Items.Add(new ComboItem(p.Id, p.Name));
                cboPriority.SelectedIndex = 0;

                // cboStatus â€” sáº¯p theo DisplayOrder tá»« DB
                cboStatus.Items.Clear();
                cboStatus.Items.Add(new ComboItem(0, "â€” Chá»n tráº¡ng thÃ¡i â€”"));
                foreach (var s in _statuses.OrderBy(s => s.DisplayOrder))
                    cboStatus.Items.Add(new ComboItem(s.Id, s.Name));
                cboStatus.SelectedIndex = 0;

                // cboCategory
                cboCategory.Items.Clear();
                cboCategory.Items.Add(new ComboItem(0, "â€” Chá»n phÃ¢n loáº¡i â€”"));
                foreach (var c in _categories.OrderBy(c => c.Name))
                    cboCategory.Items.Add(new ComboItem(c.Id, c.Name));
                cboCategory.SelectedIndex = 0;

                // cboProject
                cboProject.Items.Clear();
                cboProject.Items.Add(new ComboItem(0, "â€” Chá»n dá»± Ã¡n â€”"));
                foreach (var proj in _projects)
                    cboProject.Items.Add(new ComboItem(proj.Id, proj.Name));
                cboProject.SelectedIndex = 0;

                // cboAssignee â€” toÃ n bá»™ user active (Developer + Manager Ä‘á»u cÃ³ thá»ƒ lÃ m)
                cboAssignee.Items.Clear();
                cboAssignee.Items.Add(new ComboItem(0, "â€” ChÆ°a gÃ¡n â€”"));
                foreach (var u in _users.OrderBy(u => u.FullName))
                    cboAssignee.Items.Add(new ComboItem(u.Id, u.FullName));
                cboAssignee.SelectedIndex = 0;
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº£i dá»¯ liá»‡u dropdown:\n" + ex.Message,
                    "Lá»—i", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
            }
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // LOAD TASK Äá»‚ Sá»¬A
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private async Task LoadTaskForEditAsync(int taskId)
        {
            _editingTask = await _taskService.GetByIdAsync(taskId);

            if (_editingTask == null)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y cÃ´ng viá»‡c nÃ y. CÃ³ thá»ƒ Ä‘Ã£ bá»‹ xÃ³a.",
                    "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                this.DialogResult = DialogResult.Cancel;
                this.Close();
                return;
            }

            // â”€â”€ Äiá»n dá»¯ liá»‡u vÃ o form â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            txtTitle.Text           = _editingTask.Title;
            txtDescription.Text     = _editingTask.Description ?? string.Empty;
            numProgress.Value       = _editingTask.ProgressPercent;
            numEstimatedHours.Value = (decimal)(_editingTask.EstimatedHours ?? 0);

            if (_editingTask.DueDate.HasValue)
            {
                chkHasDueDate.Checked = true;
                dtpDueDate.Value      = _editingTask.DueDate.Value.ToLocalTime();
                dtpDueDate.Enabled    = true;
            }
            else
            {
                chkHasDueDate.Checked = false;
                dtpDueDate.Enabled    = false;
            }

            // â”€â”€ Chá»n Ä‘Ãºng item ComboBox â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            // ProjectId, PriorityId, StatusId, CategoryId: int (non-nullable) â†’ truyá»n tháº³ng
            // AssignedToId: int? (nullable) â†’ cáº§n ?? 0
            SelectComboById(cboProject,  _editingTask.ProjectId);
            SelectComboById(cboPriority, _editingTask.PriorityId);
            SelectComboById(cboStatus,   _editingTask.StatusId);
            SelectComboById(cboCategory, _editingTask.CategoryId);
            SelectComboById(cboAssignee, _editingTask.AssignedToId ?? 0);

            // â”€â”€ PHÃ‚N QUYá»€N ENABLE/DISABLE â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
            //
            // AppSession.IsManager tráº£ true khi role lÃ  "Admin" HOáº¶C "Manager"
            // (kiá»ƒm tra á»Ÿ AppSession â€” Ä‘Ã£ dÃ¹ng Contains vá»›i IgnoreCase)
            //
            // NhÆ°ng Ä‘á»ƒ cháº¯c cháº¯n, ta tá»± kiá»ƒm tra láº¡i báº±ng OrdinalIgnoreCase:
            bool isManagerOrAbove = AppSession.Roles.Any(
                r => r.Equals("Admin",   StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                     r.Equals("Manager", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

            // Developer Ä‘ang lÃ  Assignee cá»§a task nÃ y khÃ´ng?
            bool isAssignee = _editingTask.AssignedToId.HasValue
                           && _editingTask.AssignedToId.Value == AppSession.UserId;

            // cboStatus:   Admin/Manager tá»± do | Developer chá»‰ khi lÃ  assignee
            cboStatus.Enabled   = isManagerOrAbove || isAssignee;

            // cboPriority: CHá»ˆ Admin/Manager â€” Developer khÃ´ng quyáº¿t Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘á»™ Æ°u tiÃªn
            cboPriority.Enabled = isManagerOrAbove;

            // cboAssignee: Admin/Manager tá»± do | Developer chá»‰ khi lÃ  assignee
            cboAssignee.Enabled = isManagerOrAbove || isAssignee;
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // Máº¶C Äá»ŠNH KHI THÃŠM Má»šI
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private void SetDefaultsForNewTask()
        {
            // Seed: Priority Id=1 Low | Id=2 Medium | Id=3 High | Id=4 Critical
            // index 0="â€” Chá»n â€”", index 1=Low, index 2=Medium â†’ chá»n Medium lÃ m default
            if (cboPriority.Items.Count > 2)
                cboPriority.SelectedIndex = 2; // Medium

            // Seed: Status Id=1 "CREATED" â€” Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn trong danh sÃ¡ch (DisplayOrder=0)
            // index 0="â€” Chá»n â€”", index 1=CREATED
            if (cboStatus.Items.Count > 1)
                cboStatus.SelectedIndex = 1; // CREATED

            chkHasDueDate.Checked = false;
            dtpDueDate.Enabled    = false;
            dtpDueDate.Value      = DateTime.Now.AddDays(7);

            // Khi táº¡o má»›i: Enable táº¥t cáº£ (ngÆ°á»i táº¡o Ä‘Æ°á»£c quyáº¿t Ä‘á»‹nh háº¿t)
            // Ngoáº¡i lá»‡: Developer khÃ´ng set Priority
            bool isManagerOrAbove = AppSession.Roles.Any(
                r => r.Equals("Admin",   StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                     r.Equals("Manager", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

            cboStatus.Enabled   = true;
            cboPriority.Enabled = isManagerOrAbove; // Developer khÃ´ng set Priority
            cboAssignee.Enabled = true;
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // Sá»° KIá»†N
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private void chkHasDueDate_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => dtpDueDate.Enabled = chkHasDueDate.Checked;

        private void numProgress_ValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
            => chkIsCompleted.Checked = numProgress.Value == 100;

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // NÃšT LÆ¯U
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private async void btnSave_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (!ValidateInputs()) return;

            btnSave.Enabled = false;
            btnSave.Text    = "Äang lÆ°u...";

            try
            {
                var task      = BuildTaskFromForm();
                var (ok, msg) = _taskId.HasValue
                    ? await _taskService.UpdateTaskAsync(task)
                    : await _taskService.CreateTaskAsync(task);

                if (ok)
                {
                    MessageBox.Show(msg, "ThÃ nh cÃ´ng",
                        MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Information);
                    this.DialogResult = DialogResult.OK;
                    this.Close();
                }
                else
                {
                    MessageBox.Show(msg, "KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ lÆ°u",
                        MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Lá»—i khÃ´ng mong Ä‘á»£i:\n" + ex.Message,
                    "Lá»—i há»‡ thá»‘ng", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
            }
            finally
            {
                btnSave.Enabled = true;
                btnSave.Text    = "ðŸ’¾ LÆ°u";
            }
        }

        private void btnCancel_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            this.DialogResult = DialogResult.Cancel;
            this.Close();
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // VALIDATE
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private bool ValidateInputs()
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtTitle.Text))
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Vui lÃ²ng nháº­p tiÃªu Ä‘á» cÃ´ng viá»‡c.",
                    "Thiáº¿u thÃ´ng tin", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                txtTitle.Focus();
                return false;
            }
            if (txtTitle.Text.Trim().Length > 200)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("TiÃªu Ä‘á» khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c dÃ i hÆ¡n 200 kÃ½ tá»±.",
                    "TiÃªu Ä‘á» quÃ¡ dÃ i", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                txtTitle.Focus();
                return false;
            }
            if (GetComboId(cboProject) <= 0)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Vui lÃ²ng chá»n dá»± Ã¡n cho cÃ´ng viá»‡c.",
                    "Thiáº¿u thÃ´ng tin", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                cboProject.Focus();
                return false;
            }
            if (GetComboId(cboPriority) <= 0)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Vui lÃ²ng chá»n má»©c Ä‘á»™ Æ°u tiÃªn.",
                    "Thiáº¿u thÃ´ng tin", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                cboPriority.Focus();
                return false;
            }
            if (GetComboId(cboStatus) <= 0)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Vui lÃ²ng chá»n tráº¡ng thÃ¡i cÃ´ng viá»‡c.",
                    "Thiáº¿u thÃ´ng tin", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                cboStatus.Focus();
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // BUILD ENTITY Tá»ª FORM
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        private TaskItem BuildTaskFromForm()
        {
            // Sá»­a â†’ dÃ¹ng láº¡i entity gá»‘c (giá»¯ CreatedAt, CreatedById, Reviewer, Tester...)
            // ThÃªm má»›i â†’ entity rá»—ng
            var task = _editingTask ?? new TaskItem();

            task.Title       = txtTitle.Text.Trim();
            task.Description = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtDescription.Text)
                                   ? null
                                   : txtDescription.Text.Trim();

            // CÃ¡c FK int (non-nullable) â€” gÃ¡n trá»±c tiáº¿p tá»« ComboBox Id
            task.ProjectId  = GetComboId(cboProject);
            task.PriorityId = GetComboId(cboPriority);
            task.StatusId   = GetComboId(cboStatus);   // â† gÃ¡n Ä‘Ã¢y, UpdateTaskAsync sáº½
                                                        //   gá»i UpdateStatusAsync riÃªng Ä‘á»ƒ cháº¯c
            task.CategoryId = GetComboId(cboCategory);

            // AssignedToId lÃ  int? â€” Id=0 (placeholder "ChÆ°a gÃ¡n") â†’ null
            var assigneeId    = GetComboId(cboAssignee);
            task.AssignedToId = assigneeId > 0 ? assigneeId : null;

            task.ProgressPercent = (byte)numProgress.Value;
            task.IsCompleted     = chkIsCompleted.Checked;
            task.EstimatedHours  = numEstimatedHours.Value > 0
                                       ? (decimal?)numEstimatedHours.Value
                                       : null;
            task.DueDate = chkHasDueDate.Checked
                               ? dtpDueDate.Value.ToUniversalTime()
                               : null;

            // Chá»‰ gÃ¡n khi thÃªm má»›i â€” khÃ´ng ghi Ä‘Ã¨ khi sá»­a
            if (!_taskId.HasValue)
            {
                task.CreatedById = AppSession.UserId;
                task.CreatedAt   = DateTime.UtcNow;
            }

            return task;
        }

        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        // HELPERS
        // â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

        /// <summary>Láº¥y Id tá»« ComboBox; tráº£ 0 náº¿u chÆ°a chá»n (placeholder).</summary>
        private static int GetComboId(ComboBox cbo)
            => cbo.SelectedItem is ComboItem ci ? ci.Id : 0;

        /// <summary>
        /// Chá»n item trong ComboBox theo Id.
        /// Nháº­n int (non-nullable) â€” gá»i vá»›i ?? 0 cho int? (AssignedToId).
        /// </summary>
        private static void SelectComboById(ComboBox cbo, int id)
        {
            if (id <= 0) return;
            for (int i = 0; i < cbo.Items.Count; i++)
            {
                if (cbo.Items[i] is ComboItem ci && ci.Id == id)
                {
                    cbo.SelectedIndex = i;
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

    public partial class frmTaskList : Form
